### Grid square

[L-19](/wiki/Standard_Galactic_Grid "Standard Galactic Grid")[[5]](#cite_note-TFABG-5)

### Distance from Core

53,000 [light-years](/wiki/Light-year "Light-year")[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6)

### Suns

1: [Priate](/wiki/Priate "Priate")[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6)

### Orbital position

3,[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) overlapping [orbit](/wiki/Orbit "Orbit")[[7]](#cite_note-FF-7)

### Moons

1[[8]](#cite_note-CLNE-8)

### Trade routes

[Tosste Spur](/wiki/Tosste_Spur "Tosste Spur")[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6)

### Orbital period

412 [local rotations](/wiki/Local_day "Local day") (618 [standard days](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day"))[[9]](#cite_note-year_note-9)

## Physical information

### Class

* Terrestrial (historic)[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6)
* Wasteland ([Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"))[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6)

### Diameter

4,200 [kilometers](/wiki/Kilometer "Kilometer")[[2]](#cite_note-Galactic_Explorer's_Guide-2) (2,610 miles)[[10]](#cite_note-VE-10)

### Atmosphere

[Type II](/wiki/Atmosphere "Atmosphere") ([breath mask](/wiki/Breath_mask "Breath mask") suggested)[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6)

### Climate

* Temperate (historic)[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11)
* [Hot](/wiki/Temperature "Temperature"),[[12]](#cite_note-Mustafar_DB-12) ash-laden, and stormy (Imperial Era)[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13)

### Gravity

Standard[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6)

* Molten rock plains[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15)
* [Obsidian](/wiki/Obsidian "Obsidian") [mountain](/wiki/Mountain "Mountain") ranges[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) and shores[[2]](#cite_note-Galactic_Explorer's_Guide-2)

0%[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6)

:   "*I've only heard that name once. From Kanan. He said Mustafar is where Jedi go to die.*"
:   ―Hera Syndulla — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/47/Hera-Jedi-go-to-die.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250325171554)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:Hera-Jedi-go-to-die.flac "File:Hera-Jedi-go-to-die.flac"))[[32]](#cite_note-Rebel_Resolve-32)

**Mustafar** was a young, small [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") located in the [Mustafar system](/wiki/Mustafar_system "Mustafar system"), within the [Atravis sector](/wiki/Atravis_sector "Atravis sector") of [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy")'s [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories"). Once a [garden](/wiki/Plant "Plant") world nourished by the [Bright Star](/wiki/Bright_Star "Bright Star") artifact, its [orbit](/wiki/Orbit "Orbit") was shifted when [Lady](/wiki/Lady "Lady") [Corvax](/wiki/Corvax "Corvax") [unleashed](/wiki/Aeon_Engine "Aeon Engine") the energies of the Bright Star in an attempt to [return](/wiki/Immortality "Immortality") her [husband](/wiki/Dorwin_Corvax "Dorwin Corvax") to life. The resulting [gravimetric](/wiki/Gravity "Gravity") duel between the [gas giants](/wiki/Gas_giant "Gas giant") [Jestefad](/wiki/Jestefad "Jestefad") and [Lefrani](/wiki/Lefrani "Lefrani") over Mustafar [heated](/wiki/Temperature "Temperature") the planet's core, transforming the lush world into an imbalanced [volcanic](/wiki/Volcano "Volcano") [hellscape](/wiki/Chaos "Chaos"). Adapting to life on their devastated [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld"), the [arthropodal](/wiki/Arthropod "Arthropod") [Mustafarians](/wiki/Mustafarian "Mustafarian") evolved into [two](/wiki/Northern_Mustafarian "Northern Mustafarian") [distinct](/wiki/Southern_Mustafarian "Southern Mustafarian") [subspecies](/wiki/Species "Species") that cooperated to ensure their continued survival. Legends of Corvax's search for immortality brought the ancient [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") to Mustafar, seeking the same secrets of eternal life. There, they built a [temple](/wiki/Sith_temple_(Mustafar) "Sith temple (Mustafar)") over a [locus](/wiki/Vergence "Vergence") in the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"), above the buried ruins of [Corvax Fortress](/wiki/Corvax_Fortress "Corvax Fortress").

Acquired by the [Techno Union](/wiki/Techno_Union "Techno Union") over three hundred [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), Mustafar's [lava](/wiki/Magma "Magma") flows were [mined](/wiki/Mining "Mining") for unique and valuable minerals. It was also home to the [Black Sun](/wiki/Black_Sun "Black Sun") crime syndicate, whose [headquarters](/wiki/Black_Sun_fortress "Black Sun fortress") was located near the mining [town](/wiki/City "City") that became known as [Zitontown](/wiki/Zitontown "Zitontown") after the [Falleen](/wiki/Falleen "Falleen") [Ziton Moj](/wiki/Ziton_Moj "Ziton Moj") [ascended](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar_(Death_Watch) "Mission to Mustafar (Death Watch)") to leadership of the organization. As part of the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") during the Clone Wars, the Techno Union on Mustafar [produced](/wiki/Techno_Union_droid_factory "Techno Union droid factory") [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid") for the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army"). [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") had a [secret facility](/wiki/Darth_Sidious%27s_secret_facility "Darth Sidious's secret facility") on the planet where he intended to turn "[harvested](/wiki/Project_Harvester "Project Harvester")" [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") [children](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling") into [Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force")-talented [spies](/wiki/Spy "Spy"). However, the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") had the base scuttled when [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") and his [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan"), [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano"), arrived to [rescue](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar_(Skywalker_and_Tano) "Mission to Mustafar (Skywalker and Tano)") [the](/wiki/Wee_Dunn "Wee Dunn") [younglings](/wiki/Zinn_Toa "Zinn Toa").

Mustafar served as the [final redoubt](/wiki/Klegger_Corp_Mining_Facility "Klegger Corp Mining Facility") of the [Separatist Council](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council") until the newly-appointed [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Vader, formerly Anakin Skywalker, was [sent](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar") by Sidious to [slaughter](/wiki/Death "Death") the council, effectively ending the Clone Wars. The [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") was confronted by his [wife](/wiki/Marriage "Marriage"), [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala"), and his former [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master"), [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"). The latter [dueled](/wiki/Duel_on_Mustafar "Duel on Mustafar") Vader, defeating him and leaving him to burn on a lava bank. However, Vader was saved when Sidious arrived and carried him offworld. Mustafar then came under the ownership of the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") after the Techno Union and its assets were nationalized. Sidious had new facilities built on the planet, where more Force-sensitive infants were taken and transformed into agents of the [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius").

During this [era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"), Vader returned to the site of his greatest defeat and, with the help of the ancient Sith Lord [Darth Momin](/wiki/Darth_Momin "Darth Momin"), [erected](/wiki/Battle_of_Fortress_Vader "Battle of Fortress Vader") the massive monolith [Fortress Vader](/wiki/Fortress_Vader "Fortress Vader") to serve as his personal sanctum, built on the [site](/wiki/Sith_cave "Sith cave") of the former [Sith temple](/wiki/Sith_temple "Sith temple"). Throughout the Age of the Empire, Vader used the planet to fulfill his master's biddings, with the fiery world becoming the final resting place for [victims](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") of the [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge"). In addition, Vader also undertook personal business within his new realm, attempting to wield the dark powers of Mustafar to bring his deceased wife back from the dead.

Following the Dark Lord of the Sith, the Empire took hold of planet. Resource extraction efforts on Mustafar were taken over by the [Mining Guild](/wiki/Mining_Guild "Mining Guild"), although strict Imperial travel restrictions on the [system](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") made it difficult for the guild to turn a profit and mining operations eventually ceased entirely. Black Sun also abandoned Mustafar for a more low profile world when the Empire established a [garrison](/wiki/Fortress_Vader_Imperial_garrison "Fortress Vader Imperial garrison") there. The Mustafarians resisted the Imperial occupation of their homeworld and attempted to drive them from Mustafar by launching [multiple](/wiki/Raid_on_Fortress_Vader "Raid on Fortress Vader") [assaults](/wiki/Attack_on_Fortress_Vader "Attack on Fortress Vader") on Fortress Vader.

Although it hosted one of the [earliest rebel victories](/wiki/Action_at_Mustafar "Action at Mustafar") of the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War"), Mustafar fell into obscurity following Vader's demise at the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor"), though Black Sun did eventually return to the planet. After the [destruction](/wiki/Battle_on_Mustafar "Battle on Mustafar") of the Bright Star, the planet's ecosystem slowly began to heal from the devastation it had endured for [centuries](/wiki/Standard_century "Standard century") prior. Many devout pilgrims journeyed to the ruins of Fortress Vader, hoping to tap into the late Sith's dark power. [Decades](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") after Vader's death, his grandson, [Kylo Ren](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo"), [journeyed](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar_(First_Order) "Mission to Mustafar (First Order)") to the world to continue the legacy of his [family's](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family") grisly past. The [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") of the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order") slaughtered the [Sith cult](/wiki/Alazmec_of_Winsit "Alazmec of Winsit") that defended Fortress Vader and discovered his grandfather's [Sith wayfinder](/wiki/Vader%27s_wayfinder "Vader's wayfinder"), a tool that allowed him to locate the phantom [emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") Sidious on [Exegol](/wiki/Exegol "Exegol").

## Description[]

### World of fire[]

:   "*Mustafar is a lava planet, terrible place, full of awful mines. There's a custom there to jump lava flows and…well, you'll see.*"
:   ―L3-37[[33]](#cite_note-Lando's_Luck-33)

 [![The landscape of Mustafar was harsh and filled with lava.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/Acme-HighGround.png/revision/latest?cb=20250220143751) [![The landscape of Mustafar was harsh and filled with lava.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/Acme-HighGround.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20250220143751)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/Acme-HighGround.png/revision/latest?cb=20250220143751) 

The landscape of Mustafar was harsh and filled with lava.

 

Mustafar was a young[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) rocky [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") within the [eponymous system](/wiki/Mustafar_system "Mustafar system")[[4]](#cite_note-ROTS-4) of the [Atravis sector](/wiki/Atravis_sector "Atravis sector"), in the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories"). It was a small world[[34]](#cite_note-CVD-34) situated in grid square L-19[[5]](#cite_note-TFABG-5) of the [Standard Galactic Grid](/wiki/Standard_Galactic_Grid "Standard Galactic Grid"),[[35]](#cite_note-Rebel_Dossier-35) and it lay on the [Tosste Spur](/wiki/Tosste_Spur "Tosste Spur") [trade route](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route"), off the [Rimma Trade Route](/wiki/Rimma_Trade_Route "Rimma Trade Route").[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) A part of the [Western Reaches](/wiki/Western_Reaches "Western Reaches"),[[2]](#cite_note-Galactic_Explorer's_Guide-2) Mustafar was located 53,000 [light-years](/wiki/Light-year "Light-year") from [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy")'s [Core](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds").[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6)

With an overlapping [orbit](/wiki/Orbit "Orbit"),[[7]](#cite_note-FF-7) Mustafar was the third orbit of its [system](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") around the primary [star](/wiki/Star "Star") [Priate](/wiki/Priate "Priate"),[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) completing a [full rotation](/wiki/Local_day "Local day") every 36 [standard hours](/wiki/Standard_hour "Standard hour")[[2]](#cite_note-Galactic_Explorer's_Guide-2) and a revolution around its sun every 412 local days, the equivalent of 618 [standard days](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day").[[9]](#cite_note-year_note-9) It had a diameter of 4,200 [kilometers](/wiki/Kilometer "Kilometer"),[[2]](#cite_note-Galactic_Explorer's_Guide-2) or 2,610 miles,[[10]](#cite_note-VE-10) and was a terrestrial world classed as a wasteland during the Imperial Era.[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6)

Nourished by the power of the [Bright Star](/wiki/Bright_Star "Bright Star") artifact, it was once a[[14]](#cite_note-Immortal_1-14) temperate and[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11) [lush](/wiki/Plant "Plant") garden world that thrived with lifeforms that inhabited [forests](/wiki/Forest "Forest").[[14]](#cite_note-Immortal_1-14) [Millennia](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium") before the Imperial Era, Mustafar [became](/wiki/Devastation_of_Mustafar "Devastation of Mustafar") an unstable [volcanic](/wiki/Volcano "Volcano") world with underground [caves](/wiki/Cave "Cave")[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) and free-flowing[[36]](#cite_note-BMF_42-36) [lava](/wiki/Magma "Magma") constituting 35% of its[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) volatile[[36]](#cite_note-BMF_42-36) surface,[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) taking the form of lava [seas](/wiki/Ocean "Ocean"),[[16]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_novel-16) rivers,[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) and pits[[12]](#cite_note-Mustafar_DB-12) interspersed with glens, molten rock plains,[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) as well as [obsidian](/wiki/Obsidian "Obsidian") [mountain](/wiki/Mountain "Mountain") ranges[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) and shores.[[2]](#cite_note-Galactic_Explorer's_Guide-2) Few areas were temperate enough to sustain life, and only a few landmasses were not fractured by tectonic disruption and magma flows; allowing lifeforms to evolve deep underground.[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11)

The tortured planet[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) was powerful in the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"),[[37]](#cite_note-DV5-37) and, along with valuable [mineral](/wiki/Mineral "Mineral") allotropes that surfaced from the planet core[[34]](#cite_note-CVD-34) as well as its obscurity to the wider galaxy, attracted various off-world interests that exploited the molten planet.[[12]](#cite_note-Mustafar_DB-12) Mustafar remained a [fiery](/wiki/Fire "Fire") world until the destruction of the Bright Star, at which point the planet was allowed to regrow.[[38]](#cite_note-Immortal_3-38) Such different states of the world led some to believe that spiritual forces were the catalysts to the changes in Mustafar's nature.[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) Despite the planet's rugged and dangerous nature, there was a deadly beauty to the volcanic landscapes.[[39]](#cite_note-BMF_85-39)

### Heart of lava[]

:   "*Of all the fumes that drift up from the lava lakes deep underground, these were the most potent. They played tricks with your head…making you see things that weren't there. Shadows of the mind. Fears… doubts… ghosts of the past.*"
:   ―Lellis, on Mustafar's lava fumes[[27]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Vader-27)

Deep underground, Mustafar contained lava lakes from which [fumes](/wiki/Lava_fume "Lava fume") drifted up to surface-level facilities; such [fumes](/wiki/Gas "Gas") played tricks with the minds of organics who inhaled it, giving rise to what [Lellis](/wiki/Lellis "Lellis") referred to as "shadows of the mind"—visions of fears and doubts that could manifest as ghosts of the past. Lava fumes were most potent around the vicinity of the [Klegger Corp Mining Facility](/wiki/Klegger_Corp_Mining_Facility "Klegger Corp Mining Facility"), and sustained exposure to it drove an individual insane. [Repulsor vents](/wiki/Repulsor_vent "Repulsor vent") were thus installed at the Mining Complex to prevent such toxic fumes from rising to indoor facilities and being inhaled by those within.[[27]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Vader-27)

 [![Mustafar and its twin, Jestefad](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/Jestefad.png/revision/latest?cb=20130208043311) [![Mustafar and its twin, Jestefad](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/Jestefad.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/360?cb=20130208043311)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/Jestefad.png/revision/latest?cb=20130208043311) 

Mustafar and its twin, Jestefad

 

Mustafar was twinned with the [gas giant](/wiki/Gas_giant "Gas giant") [Jestefad](/wiki/Jestefad "Jestefad"), which it closely orbited, being constantly pulled by its [gravitational](/wiki/Gravity "Gravity") force; Mustafar was nearly captured by the larger world as its [moon](/wiki/Moon "Moon"), an event that was only prevented by the counterbalancing gravitational pull from the more remote gas giant [Lefrani](/wiki/Lefrani "Lefrani"). Mustafar nevertheless possessed a standard gravity. The influence of the massive magnetic field of Mustafar's larger twin, however, resulted in its [hellish](/wiki/Chaos "Chaos") volcanic landscape, as the power of Jestefad's gravitational force caused massive tidal disruption that heated Mustafar's interior.[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13)

Along with being engulfed in a constant gravimetric battle, Mustafar housed an unstable core that caused [groundquakes](/wiki/Groundquake "Groundquake") powerful enough to split the planet's continents apart,[[40]](#cite_note-TROS_JN-40) and its split tectonic plates allowed the planet's searing magma to push through to the surface, creating a volcanic hot spot visible as a bright red cluster from [space](/wiki/Realspace "Realspace").[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) Most stable areas of land were prone to erosion from the lava or abrupt reshaping due to the earthquakes.[[39]](#cite_note-BMF_85-39)

While great portions of the planet were always in motion, one of the few constant features was the [central volcano](/wiki/Central_volcano "Central volcano"). Lava poured out of the spot at nearly 100,000 [liters](/wiki/Liter "Liter") per [second](/wiki/Second "Second") and pooled at the giant volcano's base. To the north was a region named the [Burning Plains](/wiki/Burning_Plains "Burning Plains"), which boasted heavy volcanic activity. Another region earned its nickname, the [Smoking Forest](/wiki/Smoking_Forest "Smoking Forest"), as smoke spewed from its [tree](/wiki/Tree "Tree")-like rock chimneys. Mustafar's [Berken's Flow](/wiki/Berken%27s_Flow "Berken's Flow") was the largest lavafall in the galaxy, while [Tulrus Island](/wiki/Tulrus_Island "Tulrus Island")[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6)—which shared its name with the [tulrus](/wiki/Tulrus "Tulrus") creature[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11)—was surrounded by tall mountains.[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6)

 [![Mustafar featured rivers of lava.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/MustafarBackdrop-SWH.png/revision/latest?cb=20250219210501) [![Mustafar featured rivers of lava.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/MustafarBackdrop-SWH.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250219210501)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/MustafarBackdrop-SWH.png/revision/latest?cb=20250219210501) 

Mustafar featured rivers of lava.

 

The young[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) world's instability churned magma that carried [ores](/wiki/Ore "Ore")[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) with unique and valuable minerals[[41]](#cite_note-Calendar2020-41) to its surface,[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) attracting business interests[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) from various[[2]](#cite_note-Galactic_Explorer's_Guide-2) galactic [mining](/wiki/Mining "Mining") conglomerates[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) such as the [Mining Guild](/wiki/Mining_Guild "Mining Guild")[[2]](#cite_note-Galactic_Explorer's_Guide-2) to exploit the mineral wealth of the otherwise untouched world.[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) Mining facilities were set up for minerals and metal ore,[[31]](#cite_note-AEYNK-31) including [dolovite](/wiki/Dolovite "Dolovite"),[[18]](#cite_note-SW11-18) [gold](/wiki/Gold "Gold"),[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) and [mirkanite](/wiki/Mirkanite "Mirkanite").[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6)

The searing magma that bubbled beneath the surface flooded the planet, covering it in oceans[[16]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_novel-16) and rivers of lava. Geothermal energy was the main power source of the [Techno Union](/wiki/Techno_Union "Techno Union")'s mining complex on the planet,[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) and the lava flows that coated the rocky terrain left behind traces of [flood basalt](/wiki/Flood_basalt "Flood basalt").[[42]](#cite_note-DV21-42) At 800°C (1500[°F](/wiki/%C2%B0F "°F")), Mustafar's lava, while still very hot, had a lower [temperature](/wiki/Temperature "Temperature") than that found on other worlds due to unusual mineral allotropes that were molten at lower temperatures.[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) Nevertheless, patches of Mustafar began to cool in the [decades](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") leading up to[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY").[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43)

### Tempestuous skies[]

 [![The electromagnetic interference in Mustafar's atmosphere posed a risk to travelers.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/FDKF_FC_BG_art.png/revision/latest?cb=20181001025016) [![The electromagnetic interference in Mustafar's atmosphere posed a risk to travelers.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/FDKF_FC_BG_art.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20181001025016)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/FDKF_FC_BG_art.png/revision/latest?cb=20181001025016) 

The electromagnetic interference in Mustafar's atmosphere posed a risk to travelers.

 

Mustafar's atmosphere was influenced by the breath of its volcanoes and Jestefad's massive magnetic field. Along with cyclonic-force updrafts and thermal currents, titanic lightning storms made up the planet's unfriendly skies. Turbulent and ash-laden,[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) the atmosphere was also hot and chemical,[[44]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-44) consisting of thick clouds of black smoke[[21]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-21) and allowing for[[40]](#cite_note-TROS_JN-40) choking ash[[31]](#cite_note-AEYNK-31) to fall like rain.[[40]](#cite_note-TROS_JN-40) Lava processing operations created toxic gas by-products,[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) and a noxious air cast the world in a hazy fog.[[44]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-44) Thus, Mustafar was classified as a world with a Type II atmosphere, wherein the usage of a [breath mask](/wiki/Breath_mask "Breath mask") was recommended.[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6)

The frequent[[34]](#cite_note-CVD-34) electromagnetic interference and lightning storms in the atmosphere respectively led to signal loss and noise, although the effects of Mustafar's hectic skies could be reduced through the use of dedicated dampers.[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) The planet's magnetic field interfered with [sensors](/wiki/Sensor "Sensor") installed on the surface,[[45]](#cite_note-CR_4-45) and electromagnetic interference also posed a significant risk for off-world arrivals and departures.[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) Those caught in one such storm[[42]](#cite_note-DV21-42) without the assistance of specially shielded surface-level landing equipment[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13)—which included energy-shielded[[34]](#cite_note-CVD-34) landing pads and [guidance](/wiki/Guide_beam "Guide beam") and [tractor beams](/wiki/Tractor_beam "Tractor beam")—found, at best, their [starship](/wiki/Starship "Starship")'s scanners rendered useless and navigational equipment and control systems interfered with.[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) In certain cases, a ship was torn apart[[42]](#cite_note-DV21-42) as Mustafar was by Lefrani and Jestefad.[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) Ships were additionally threatened by Mustafar's intense heat and incendiary ash, although any damage could be prevented should a vessel be equipped with sufficiently powerful [energy shields](/wiki/Deflector_shield_generator "Deflector shield generator").[[46]](#cite_note-CV-46)

### Fauna and flora[]

#### Hardy beasts[]

##### Lethal predators[]

 [![The cavernous underground of Mustafar was home to ferocious creatures (darkghast pictured).](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/21/Darkghast-art.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230705174535) [![The cavernous underground of Mustafar was home to ferocious creatures (darkghast pictured).](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/21/Darkghast-art.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20230705174535)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/21/Darkghast-art.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230705174535) 

The cavernous underground of Mustafar was home to ferocious creatures (darkghast pictured).

 

Despite the hellish environment after its devastation, Mustafar was teeming with life, a home to fragile but determined organisms all connected through [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force") energy field.[[44]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-44) All surviving lifeforms had evolved deep underground, in the few areas that remained temperate and with landmasses were not fractured:[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11) in the solid rock betwixt lava flows lived [mammalian](/wiki/Mammal "Mammal"), [reptilian](/wiki/Reptile "Reptile"), and [insect](/wiki/Insect "Insect") [species](/wiki/Species "Species"),[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) although reptilian and [insectoid](/wiki/Insectoid "Insectoid") lifeforms proved to be the most successful survivors, aggressive in nature and with tough skin or carapaces.[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11) The extremophile creatures of the planet had adapted to Mustafar's desolation and become indomitable.[[44]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-44) The [sentient](/wiki/Sentience "Sentience") [Mustafarians](/wiki/Mustafarian "Mustafarian") were insectoid,[[26]](#cite_note-AEYNTK_UE-26) and were forced to live largely underground in Mustafar's north and near the equator.[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24)

Much like the planet itself, some of the creatures found on Mustafar were especially deadly.[[22]](#cite_note-Immortal_2-22) Highly aggressive creatures posed a significant hazard on the planet due to its scarce resources.[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24) The planet's apex predator was the [scorpion](/wiki/Scorpion "Scorpion")-like [Sher Kar](/wiki/Sher_Kar "Sher Kar"), which lived deep in the nesting grounds of their tulrus prey.[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11) The fearsome [darkghast](/wiki/Darkghast "Darkghast"), similar in some respects[[22]](#cite_note-Immortal_2-22) to the [rancors](/wiki/Rancor "Rancor") of the planet [Dathomir](/wiki/Dathomir "Dathomir"),[[47]](#cite_note-CE_UE-47) was a multi-[limbed](/wiki/Limb "Limb") [carnivore](/wiki/Diet "Diet") that dwelled beneath the world's rocky surface.[[22]](#cite_note-Immortal_2-22)

The reptillian [blistmok](/wiki/Blistmok "Blistmok") hunted in packs and were capable of pursuing their prey for days.[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11) The insectoid [xandanks](/wiki/Xandank "Xandank") were well protected by their armor and[[48]](#cite_note-GA-48) hunted in packs as well.[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11) Tough, semi-sentient creatures[[49]](#cite_note-HC33-49) named [roggwarts](/wiki/Roggwart "Roggwart") hunted the planet's tunnels and lava tubes in search of xandanks,[[50]](#cite_note-Cyborgs-50) as well as for giant, [human](/wiki/Human "Human")-eating[[18]](#cite_note-SW11-18) [lava eels](/wiki/Lava_eel "Lava eel"). Despite the danger of roggwarts, they could be domesticated with the proper training[[50]](#cite_note-Cyborgs-50) and were imported to Mustafar to work in the planet's mines.[[26]](#cite_note-AEYNTK_UE-26)

By [3 BBY](/wiki/3_BBY "3 BBY"), a roggwart named [Kongo](/wiki/Kongo "Kongo") the Disembowler was employed to keep the [dolovite mine](/wiki/Dolovite_mines_of_Mustafar "Dolovite mines of Mustafar") tunnels free[[48]](#cite_note-GA-48) of xandanks and lava eels.[[18]](#cite_note-SW11-18) Kongo was reputedly the last of his kind[[49]](#cite_note-HC33-49) by [0 ABY](/wiki/0_ABY "0 ABY"),[[51]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_11_date-51) although it may have been said in an effort to make the roggwart seem more mysterious and exotic.[[49]](#cite_note-HC33-49)

##### Creatures with other diets[]

:   "*The very* beasts themselves *conspire to thwart my vision. Fascinating. Utterly fascinating.*"
:   ―Lord Momin, reacting to a lava flea attack on Fortress Vader[[20]](#cite_note-DV23-20)

 [![Northern Mustafarians ride lava fleas along a molten river.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/Lava-fleas-walking.png/revision/latest?cb=20200716003228) [![Northern Mustafarians ride lava fleas along a molten river.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/Lava-fleas-walking.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/320?cb=20200716003228)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/Lava-fleas-walking.png/revision/latest?cb=20200716003228) 

Northern Mustafarians ride lava fleas along a molten river.

 

The large insectoids known as [lava fleas](/wiki/Lava_flea "Lava flea") had developed a tough exoskeleton that protected them from the world's fiery devastation.[[31]](#cite_note-AEYNK-31) They lived largely underground[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11) and ate away at the planet's crust,[[31]](#cite_note-AEYNK-31) feeding on the surface's rich minerals, rocks, and dirt and were commonly used as domesticated mounts by the sentient Mustafarians. Lava fleas and Mustafarians thus had a close connection and were the only species that thrived on Mustafar.[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11)

The large, lumbering egg-laying tulrus had sharp tusks and bad temper, while the small [jundak](/wiki/Jundak "Jundak") parasite attached itself to a host and eventually burst out, killing the host and developing into a large adult.[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11) [Lizard-crows](/wiki/Lizard-crow "Lizard-crow") occupied Mustafar's lava fields; these creatures were often scared away by what the Mustafarians referred to as "[molten men](/wiki/Molten_man "Molten man")."[[25]](#cite_note-Return_5-25) [Spark-roaches](/wiki/Spark-roach "Spark-roach")[[27]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Vader-27) and [rodents](/wiki/Rodent "Rodent") called [fire rats](/wiki/Fire_rat "Fire rat") also called Mustafar their home, the latter of which gnawed on the [lava crystals](/wiki/Lava_crystal "Lava crystal") that formed on the planet.[[23]](#cite_note-Return_1-23) A species of thick-skinned ant native to the world was known for its painful bite, which left behind burning pustules not unlike the volcanos that painted the planet's surface.[[52]](#cite_note-Beware_the_Nameless-52)

[Lava nymphs](/wiki/Lava_nymph "Lava nymph") were winged creatures that inhabited the planet's caverns in hives. Considered to be vermin, the creatures' insides were filled with lava, which they were able to spit out when provoked.[[22]](#cite_note-Immortal_2-22) Feeding on minerals, hives of [kubaza beetles](/wiki/Kubaza_beetle "Kubaza beetle") lived near lava flows and were fierce defenders of their nests;[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11) starting life as a small [larva](/wiki/Larva "Larva"), the creature developed a defense mechanism by the time it reached adulthood that allowed it to warn its brood by exploding.[[53]](#cite_note-Tales_2-53) Burrowing quadrupeds known as [krishels](/wiki/Krishel "Krishel") inhabited Mustafar's labyrinthine caverns and tunnels. Those strong, hard-shelled creatures were hunted by the Mustafarians.[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24)

#### Plants and fungi[]

 [![Irontrees were some of the few plants found on the world.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/Corvax-Fen-TROS-VD.png/revision/latest?cb=20200825134426) [![Irontrees were some of the few plants found on the world.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/Corvax-Fen-TROS-VD.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/320?cb=20200825134426)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/Corvax-Fen-TROS-VD.png/revision/latest?cb=20200825134426) 

Irontrees were some of the few plants found on the world.

 

Although the lush vegetation that once covered the planet eventually disappeared beneath fire and ash,[[14]](#cite_note-Immortal_1-14) Mustafar was not devoid of [fungal](/wiki/Fungus "Fungus") and [vegetal](/wiki/Vegetable "Vegetable") life. Hidden away from the world's searing lava rivers, [kahel cave fungi](/wiki/Kahel_cave_fungus "Kahel cave fungus") grew underground. These organisms were deeply symbolic to the native Mustafarians and served as the inspiration for their [mushroom](/wiki/Mushroom "Mushroom")-like architecture.[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) Following the destruction of the [Aeon Engine](/wiki/Aeon_Engine "Aeon Engine") during the Imperial Era,[[54]](#cite_note-Inside_Intel-54) the muggy [marshland](/wiki/Swamp "Swamp") of[[40]](#cite_note-TROS_JN-40) [Corvax Fen](/wiki/Corvax_Fen "Corvax Fen") developed near Fortress Vader,[[54]](#cite_note-Inside_Intel-54) and life began to slowly creep back once again.[[38]](#cite_note-Immortal_3-38) By 35 [ABY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"),[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) barren [irontrees](/wiki/Irontree "Irontree") stood in the few places where fertile soil existed, including the fen.[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15)

## History[]

### Cataclysm immortalized[]

:   "*Once, our world Mustafar was green, filled with life.*"
:   ―The Priestess teaches Mustafar's past to the descendant of Lady Corvax[[14]](#cite_note-Immortal_1-14)

 [![A battle (pictured) on the forest world of Mustafar claimed the life of Lord Corvax, prompting Lady Corvax to steal the Bright Star.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/CorvaxsDeath.png/revision/latest?cb=20210319021001) [![A battle (pictured) on the forest world of Mustafar claimed the life of Lord Corvax, prompting Lady Corvax to steal the Bright Star.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/CorvaxsDeath.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20210319021001)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/CorvaxsDeath.png/revision/latest?cb=20210319021001) 

A battle (pictured) on the forest world of Mustafar claimed the life of Lord Corvax, prompting Lady Corvax to steal the Bright Star.

 

In its ancient past,[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) Mustafar was a lush and [forested](/wiki/Forest "Forest")[[14]](#cite_note-Immortal_1-14) terrestrial planet,[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) thriving with life through the Bright Star, the native Mustafarians' most sacred artifact that nourished[[14]](#cite_note-Immortal_1-14) the small[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) garden world.[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) It housed an [enclave](/wiki/Jedi_enclave_(Mustafar) "Jedi enclave (Mustafar)") of the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi"),[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11) servants of the Force,[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) that drew attention from the Jedi's enemy, the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith"). After a thousand [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") of skirmishes between the two groups, they came to a titanic battle in the Mustafar system that brought havoc to Jestefad, Lefrani, and Mustafar five thousand years before the Imperial Era.[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11)

Ancient legends said that offworlders led by [Lady](/wiki/Lady "Lady") [Corvax](/wiki/Corvax "Corvax") and her [husband](/wiki/Dorwin_Corvax "Dorwin Corvax") arrived at some point, living in harmony with the natives, but the garden world was [attacked](/wiki/Attack_on_Mustafar "Attack on Mustafar") and Corvax's husband fell in battle against the invaders. Unable to let go of her love, Corvax stole the Mustafarians' Bright Star in her pursuit of [immortality](/wiki/Immortality "Immortality"), having thought it had the power to resurrect her husband from [death](/wiki/Death "Death"). Corvax created the Aeon Engine and encased the artifact within, although her actions ultimately resulted in the devastation of the planet;[[14]](#cite_note-Immortal_1-14) energies ruptured from the Bright Star, pushing Mustafar out of its original orbit.[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) Other legends claimed that due to a cataclysmic struggle between the Sith and the Jedi, the orbit of[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) the gas giant Lefrani was also shifted, and Mustafar entered an unusual and gravitationally crushing alignment between[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24) it and Jestefad's magnetic fields.[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6)

With the [devastation of Mustafar](/wiki/Devastation_of_Mustafar "Devastation of Mustafar"), the world's new, precarious orbit rendered it a volcanic wasteland[[14]](#cite_note-Immortal_1-14) as both gas giants pulled on tiny Mustafar, heating its interior in their attempts to claim Mustafar as their moon.[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) The crust of the smaller world was also torn apart, allowing the flow of lava toward the planet surface.[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) Very few species survived the cataclysm,[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24) with the homes of nearly all native species being destroyed. The remaining life-forms evolved[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) deep underground, in the few areas temperate and stable enough to support life,[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11) and developed short, tough bodies to endure the superheated clime,[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) and the Mustafarians were forced to areas in Mustafar's north and near the equator. There, they adapted and evolved to the new realities of life on Mustafar.[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24)

These events passed into legend, attracting Sith who were looking for the secrets of eternal life. Eventually, a [Sith shrine](/wiki/Sith_cave "Sith cave") was built[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) on the world's [Gahenn Plains](/wiki/Gahenn_Plains "Gahenn Plains")[[20]](#cite_note-DV23-20) as part of a [Sith temple](/wiki/Sith_temple_(Mustafar) "Sith temple (Mustafar)"),[[55]](#cite_note-USWNE-55) at the site of Lady Corvax's underground [castle](/wiki/Corvax_Fortress "Corvax Fortress").[[14]](#cite_note-Immortal_1-14) The Jedi had been forced to abandone their enclave on Mustafar following its devastation, and the world was used by a Force organization named the [Blackguard](/wiki/Blackguard_(Mustafar) "Blackguard (Mustafar)"). At some point, a Jedi and another individual fought a Sher Kar on Mustafar.[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11)

### A colony for mines and an outlaws' cove (c. 300–22 BBY)[]

 [![Mustafar's surface transformed into a hellish landscape.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Mustafar_DB.png/revision/latest?cb=20251122020921) [![Mustafar's surface transformed into a hellish landscape.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Mustafar_DB.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/266?cb=20251122020921)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Mustafar_DB.png/revision/latest?cb=20251122020921) 

Mustafar's surface transformed into a hellish landscape.

 

Over three hundred years before the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), the Techno Union came to own the planet[[34]](#cite_note-CVD-34) due to its mining interests. Mustafar was a typical mining world of a Republic Era that was dominated by large-scale commerce and industry—volcanic, profitable, and dangerous. Although volcanic worlds like Mustafar were convenient for mining due to the naturally occurring furnace, but the savings could quickly be eaten up elsewhere.[[39]](#cite_note-BMF_85-39) The Techno Union built giant mining stations[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11) at key locations[[39]](#cite_note-BMF_85-39) across Mustafar, where much of the ore extraction was done through heavily automated electromagnetic processes, and they led to valuable elements congealing as scum on top of the lava.[[11]](#cite_note-BMF_33-11) Many of such facilities were located at deep, fast-flowing lava rivers, as they could be scanned for passing ores or tapped by multi-prong collector arms. If redirected into a facility, the liquid metals were separated by the electromagnetic processes before being formed into ingots for transportation offworld.[[39]](#cite_note-BMF_85-39) The corporation provided the Mustafarians with tools to mine mineral allotropes for them,[[34]](#cite_note-CVD-34) labor which served to pay the rent that the Union charged.[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15)

[Mixed](/wiki/Colonist "Colonist") with workers of a great variety of other species, Mustafarian miners lived in simple residences at dedicated[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) rough-and-ready[[39]](#cite_note-BMF_85-39) mining towns, many of which were run-down. In addition to this,[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) the lack of water on the planet posed issues particularly for miners coming from offworld. Despite many of the miners being local, a fair amount came from other places in the galaxy and did not have the hardened nature to deal with the intense heat. The lack of water on the planet thus posed several issues, particularly for offworlders. Although water shortages were common, it did not stop the miners from brewing their own [hooch](/wiki/Alcohol "Alcohol") that was popular among the locals.[[39]](#cite_note-BMF_85-39) Miners rode lava fleas[[21]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-21)[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) or were helped by Techno Union technology for transportation.[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24)

While Mustafar was similar to other mining planets in some ways, it also had unique qualities. Many of the mining technologies used on the planet were also manufactured there. Smart smugglers and independent spacers knew this fact. Part of the wealth of mining was shared by such individuals, who could make credits transporting workers or resources. Many of Mustafar's mining companies also used their own shipping companies. Visiting ship [captains](/wiki/Captain "Captain") needed to be aware of which outposts they visited, as some were not designed with offworlder's safety in mind.[[39]](#cite_note-BMF_85-39)

While bigger installations manned by offworlders required extensive plant shielding, other, smaller ones rarely had these protections, as local Mustafarians often made use of individual lava flea armor instead. Modern mining facilities required plant shields, as even the strongest alloys and protective gear would not last long without them. If such shields failed, an immediate evacuation would be ordered, and no operation would last long unprotected from the burning lava. Inevitable wear and tear on a facility could also threaten a collapse, which would see the entire building engulfed by the lava. On the occasion of a volcanic eruption damaging a town, residents would likely be stranded if their ships were harmed, with no choice but to work as miners to earn enough to leave Mustafar.[[39]](#cite_note-BMF_85-39)

The Trade Union supplied Mustafarians with technology such as the [Baktoid](/wiki/Baktoid_Armor_Workshop "Baktoid Armor Workshop") [UH-XH](/wiki/UH-XH_Heavy_Work_Platform "UH-XH Heavy Work Platform") [repulsorlift](/wiki/Repulsorlift "Repulsorlift")-powered platforms,[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24) lava-processing centrifuges,[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) [electrorefining droids](/wiki/Electrorefining_droid "Electrorefining droid"),[[10]](#cite_note-VE-10) and the [DLC-13 mining droid](/wiki/DLC-13_mining_droid "DLC-13 mining droid")[[31]](#cite_note-AEYNK-31) to collect mineral-rich lava spewing from Mustafar's heated interior,[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) with the [ore extraction droid](/wiki/Ore_extraction_droid "Ore extraction droid") also seeing use.[[4]](#cite_note-ROTS-4) Minerals were transported across the galaxy to words such as [Nal Hutta](/wiki/Nal_Hutta "Nal Hutta"), where a shipment infested with Mustafarian ants found its way into the hands of [Churo](/wiki/Churo "Churo") the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt")[[52]](#cite_note-Beware_the_Nameless-52) in [228 BBY](/wiki/228_BBY "228 BBY").[[56]](#cite_note-Beware_the_Nameless_Date-56) Over the [centuries](/wiki/Standard_century "Standard century"), Mustafarians became wary of technology that[[34]](#cite_note-CVD-34) failed under the intense heat of their world and which had an inadequate melting point, having been witness to mechanical breakdowns. Such was the case for [speeders](/wiki/Speeder "Speeder"), including the heavy-duty UH-XH, which were generally left to be operated by [droids](/wiki/Droid "Droid").[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24) Nevertheless, by the Clone Wars' end, Mustafar had served as a literal gold mine for the Techno Union for almost three hundred standard years.[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13)

[Damask Holdings](/wiki/Damask_Holdings "Damask Holdings") also established a presence on Mustafar through a base.[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) In addition to its mining activities, desperate offworlders and law-evaders who were undeterred by the world's harsh conditions were drawn to Mustafar as a result of the obscure world's sparse population.[[12]](#cite_note-Mustafar_DB-12) Mustafar was also ideal for hiding or disposing items in secret.[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6) On the world [Felucia](/wiki/Felucia "Felucia"), an [individual](/wiki/Unidentified_individual_(Qui-Gon_Jinn) "Unidentified individual (Qui-Gon Jinn)") romantically involved with the Jedi Padawan [Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn "Qui-Gon Jinn") in [60 BBY](/wiki/60_BBY "60 BBY")[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) gifted him a rare [Mustafar fire diamond](/wiki/Mustafar_fire_diamond "Mustafar fire diamond").[[57]](#cite_note-M&A-57) In [40 BBY](/wiki/40_BBY "40 BBY"),[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) [jewel](/wiki/Gemstone "Gemstone") [thieves](/wiki/Thief "Thief") [Pax Maripher](/wiki/Pax_Maripher "Pax Maripher") and [Rahara Wick](/wiki/Rahara_Wick "Rahara Wick") discussed whether they should collect Mustafar fire diamonds, with Wick dreading the notion of doing so, before deciding to travel to the planet [Pijal](/wiki/Pijal "Pijal") for [kyber crystals](/wiki/Kyber_crystal "Kyber crystal") instead.[[57]](#cite_note-M&A-57)

### Revenge of the Sith (22–19 BBY)[]

#### Scum and villainy[]

##### Schemes in the shadows[]

:   "*I sense something, Master. And I don't like it.*"  
    "*It's the dark side, Ahsoka. This is the right place.*"
:   ―Ahsoka Tano and Anakin Skywalker — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bf/TheDarkSide-CotF.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250328200328)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:TheDarkSide-CotF.flac "File:TheDarkSide-CotF.flac"))[[17]](#cite_note-Children_of_the_Force-17)

 [![Mustafar was a haven for crime, home to the leadership of Black Sun (pictured).](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/BlackSunLeaders-Eminence.png/revision/latest?cb=20131024185422) [![Mustafar was a haven for crime, home to the leadership of Black Sun (pictured).](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/BlackSunLeaders-Eminence.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/320?cb=20131024185422)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/BlackSunLeaders-Eminence.png/revision/latest?cb=20131024185422) 

Mustafar was a haven for crime, home to the leadership of Black Sun (pictured).

 

During the Clone Wars, the Mustafarians aligned themselves with the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"). However, they were not fanatically committed to the cause, having only joined to secure themselves Separatist contracts, and life continued much as it had before. With members of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"), the [galaxy](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy")'s guardians of peace and justice, focused on defeating the Separatists, [law enforcement](/wiki/Law_enforcement_agency "Law enforcement agency") found itself in a declining state, especially in the infrequently patrolled Outer Rim. Organized crime thus flourished, such as the [Black Sun](/wiki/Black_Sun "Black Sun") syndicate led by [Falleen](/wiki/Falleen "Falleen") [nobles](/wiki/Noble "Noble") with interplanetary influence.[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24)

The Falleen operated clandestinely,[[58]](#cite_note-BS_DB-58) establishing elusive holdings on Mustafar[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24) and headquartering themselves in a well-defended [fortress](/wiki/Black_Sun_fortress "Black Sun fortress"),[[58]](#cite_note-BS_DB-58) where they regularly met[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24) and found the surrounding lava useful for the disposal of evidence.[[21]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-21) The native Mustafarians cared little for Black Sun, since most of their operations took place elsewhere in the galaxy.[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24) Hidden away from prying eyes, the Techno Union also [produced](/wiki/Techno_Union_droid_factory "Techno Union droid factory") [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid") behind their Mustafarian mining operations, situated within the same mountain as their Klegger Corp Mining Facility, at the time of the Clone Wars. By the time of the war, Darth Sidious was familiar with the existence of the Sith temple[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) at the Gahenn Plains.[[55]](#cite_note-USWNE-55)

 [![Darth Sidious maintained a secret facility on Mustafar that was intended to train kidnapped Force-sensitive children.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e6/SidiousMustafarLab-CotF.png/revision/latest?cb=20120829231855) [![Darth Sidious maintained a secret facility on Mustafar that was intended to train kidnapped Force-sensitive children.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e6/SidiousMustafarLab-CotF.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20120829231855)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e6/SidiousMustafarLab-CotF.png/revision/latest?cb=20120829231855) 

Darth Sidious maintained a secret facility on Mustafar that was intended to train kidnapped Force-sensitive children.

 

Aside from skirmishes and lesser operations, fighting largely passed Mustafar by during the Clone Wars,[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24) resulting in the planet retaining a reputation as a remote astronomical object that individuals usually only stopped on to [refuel](/wiki/Fuel "Fuel"). Nevertheless, the planet bore witness to a [plot](/wiki/Mission_to_Black_Stall_Station "Mission to Black Stall Station") to kidnap [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") [children](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling") by [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Cad Bane](/wiki/Cad_Bane "Cad Bane"), who was under the employ of the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"). Traveling on his [starfighter](/wiki/Rogue-class_Porax-38_starfighter "Rogue-class Porax-38 starfighter"), the *[Xanadu Blood](/wiki/Xanadu_Blood "Xanadu Blood")*, Bane deposited the children at Sidious' secret [facility](/wiki/Darth_Sidious%27s_secret_facility "Darth Sidious's secret facility"), where the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") planned to create an army of [spies](/wiki/Spy "Spy") strong in the Force. The two children, the [Gungan](/wiki/Gungan "Gungan") [Roo-Roo Page](/wiki/Roo-Roo_Page "Roo-Roo Page") and the [Rodian](/wiki/Rodian "Rodian") [Wee Dunn](/wiki/Wee_Dunn "Wee Dunn"), were to be prepared for a surgical procedure meant to enhance them, as Sidious aimed at having an army of Sith spies to counteract the Jedi. Upon reading through the captured *Xanadu Blood*'s fuel logs, Jedi Padawan [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano") reasoned the world could be where Bane deposited the kidnapped children so she and her [mentor](/wiki/Teacher "Teacher"), [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), traveled to Mustafar to [rescue](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar_(Skywalker_and_Tano) "Mission to Mustafar (Skywalker and Tano)") the children. As the Jedi arrived at the facility, Darth Sidious ordered the [nanny droids](/wiki/RO-series_childcare_and_nanny_droid "RO-series childcare and nanny droid") to destroy the installation so as to ensure the loss of any evidence of the plot. The [nanny droids](/wiki/Nanny_droid "Nanny droid") attempted to relocate the children, but Skywalker and Tano managed to rescue them as the facility sank into the lava lake below it.[[17]](#cite_note-Children_of_the_Force-17)

In [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"),[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) renegade Sith Lord [Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul"), his [apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") [Savage Opress](/wiki/Savage_Opress "Savage Opress"), and [Pre Vizsla](/wiki/Pre_Vizsla "Pre Vizsla"), the leader of the [Mandalorian](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian") [terrorist](/wiki/Terrorist "Terrorist") organization [Death Watch](/wiki/Death_Watch "Death Watch"), [traveled](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar_(Death_Watch) "Mission to Mustafar (Death Watch)") to the Black Sun fortress with the intention of recruiting them to their newly founded criminal empire, the [Shadow Collective](/wiki/Shadow_Collective "Shadow Collective").[[29]](#cite_note-Eminence-29) As four [*Kom'rk*-class fighter/transports](/wiki/Kom%27rk-class_fighter/transport "Kom'rk-class fighter/transport") landed outside the fortress, the [Captain of the Guard](/wiki/Captain_of_the_Guard "Captain of the Guard"),[[3]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-3) [Ziton Moj](/wiki/Ziton_Moj "Ziton Moj"), greeted them upon their arrival. With both Maul and Moj backed by large amounts of soldiers, the renegade Sith requested a meeting with the Black Sun's leaders, which Moj agreed to. The syndicate was headed by[[29]](#cite_note-Eminence-29) the Falleen [Xomit Grunseit](/wiki/Xomit_Grunseit "Xomit Grunseit"), who hailed from Mustafar.[[59]](#cite_note-TCWCE-59) After negotiations with the leaders went sour, Savage beheaded all of them with his [lightsaber](/wiki/Savage_Opress%27s_lightsaber "Savage Opress's lightsaber"). Moj became Black Sun's new leader and agreed to join the Shadow Collective, providing them with [weapons](/wiki/Weapon "Weapon"), [soldiers](/wiki/Soldier "Soldier"), and supplies. Shadow Collective forces then began to load all of the supplies the Black Sun had at their disposal onto ships.[[29]](#cite_note-Eminence-29)

##### The lost children[]

:   "*Ah, yes, scenic Mustafar, because everyone looks good in red lighting. Become a bounty hunter, see the galaxy!*"
:   ―Quinlan Vos, to Asajj Ventress[[21]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-21)

 [![Quinlan Vos and Asajj Ventress were hired by the Pykes to conduct a rescue mission at Black Sun's headquarters.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/BlackSunfortressMustafar.png/revision/latest?cb=20131024153118) [![Quinlan Vos and Asajj Ventress were hired by the Pykes to conduct a rescue mission at Black Sun's headquarters.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/BlackSunfortressMustafar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20131024153118)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/BlackSunfortressMustafar.png/revision/latest?cb=20131024153118) 

Quinlan Vos and Asajj Ventress were hired by the Pykes to conduct a rescue mission at Black Sun's headquarters.

 

When [Quinlan Vos](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos "Quinlan Vos") was sent undercover as a bounty hunter to work alongside Dooku's former apprentice, [Asajj Ventress](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress "Asajj Ventress"), the pair was hired by the [Pyke Syndicate](/wiki/Pyke_Syndicate "Pyke Syndicate") to [retrieve](/wiki/Rescue_of_Marg_Krim%27s_family "Rescue of Marg Krim's family") [Marg Krim](/wiki/Marg_Krim "Marg Krim")'s wife, [Tezzka Krim](/wiki/Tezzka_Krim "Tezzka Krim"), and their children, [Vram](/wiki/Vram_(Pyke) "Vram (Pyke)") and [Laalee](/wiki/Laalee "Laalee"), who were kidnapped by Black Sun and brought to their base on Mustafar in order to bribe the [Pykes](/wiki/Pyke "Pyke") into joining Maul's Shadow Collective. The two traveled to Mustafar in Ventress' ship, the [*Banshee*](/wiki/Banshee_(starship) "Banshee (starship)"), and entered [Zitontown](/wiki/Zitontown "Zitontown"), where they sought to gather information at the lone bar in the town, named [The Last Resort](/wiki/The_Last_Resort "The Last Resort"). Inside, the pair interrogated a [Falleen Black Sun enforcer](/wiki/Unidentified_Black_Sun_guard "Unidentified Black Sun guard") and discovered where the [prisoners](/wiki/Prisoner "Prisoner") were held. They infiltrated the lava-surrounded Black Sun fortress and rescued the children, although they later discovered that their mother was held in [Ziton's palace](/wiki/Ziton%27s_palace "Ziton's palace"). After the pair freed Tezzka, Moj had mobilized his forces for departure from Mustafar to attack the Pykes on the planet [Oba Diah](/wiki/Oba_Diah "Oba Diah").[[21]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-21)

#### Mirror of the soul[]

##### The obviated war[]

:   "*After you have killed all the Jedi in the Temple, go to the Mustafar system. Wipe out Viceroy Gunray and the other Separatist leaders. Once more the Sith will rule the galaxy, and we shall have peace…*"
:   ―Darth Sidious to his new apprentice, Darth Vader — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/Sidious-we-shall-have-peace.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250403185203)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:Sidious-we-shall-have-peace.flac "File:Sidious-we-shall-have-peace.flac"))[[4]](#cite_note-ROTS-4)

 [![The Mustafarian mining complex that served as the Separatist Council's refuge at the war's end.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2e/KleggerCorpMiningFacility.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210052026) [![The Mustafarian mining complex that served as the Separatist Council's refuge at the war's end.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2e/KleggerCorpMiningFacility.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/320?cb=20130210052026)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2e/KleggerCorpMiningFacility.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210052026) 

The Mustafarian mining complex that served as the Separatist Council's refuge at the war's end.

 

As the war's end drew nearer, Darth Sidious instructed the [Separatist Council](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council") to retreat to their facility on Mustafar, and they gathered at the Techno Union's Klegger Corp Mining Facility under the leadership of [Viceroy](/wiki/Viceroy_of_the_Trade_Federation "Viceroy of the Trade Federation") [Nute Gunray](/wiki/Nute_Gunray "Nute Gunray"). Soon afterward, the Jedi Anakin Skywalker made a [pact](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") with Sidious, becoming his new Sith apprentice, [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Vader; the Jedi-turned-Sith was desperately hoping to gain the power to save his lover and [wife](/wiki/Marriage "Marriage"), Republic [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala"), from dying. Darth Vader's first mission was to [eliminate](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar") Separatist leaders on Mustafar.[[4]](#cite_note-ROTS-4)

Traveling from the Republic [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") world of Coruscant in his [interceptor](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_green_Eta-2_Actis-class_interceptor "Darth Vader's green Eta-2 Actis-class interceptor") alongside his [droid](/wiki/Astromech_droid "Astromech droid") [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2"), Vader arrived at the Separatist facility's war room and promptly slaughtered the Separatist Council and their guards, bathing in the power of the dark side. At his [master's](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master") command, Vader further transmitted the order to deactivate the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army") immediately, effectively ending the Clone Wars. At the same time, the Republic's [clone army](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic") was ordered to kill all Jedi, and Darth Sidious took the opportunity to [found](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") with himself as the [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor"), fulfilling the Sith [Grand Plan](/wiki/Grand_Plan "Grand Plan") with his aim to seize control of the galaxy.[[4]](#cite_note-ROTS-4)

 [![Lefrani eclipses Mustafar's sun, just after Darth Vader's massacre of the Separatists.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/Lefranieclipse.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215033830) [![Lefrani eclipses Mustafar's sun, just after Darth Vader's massacre of the Separatists.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/Lefranieclipse.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/320?cb=20130215033830)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/Lefranieclipse.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215033830) 

Lefrani eclipses Mustafar's sun, just after Darth Vader's massacre of the Separatists.

 

A rumor spread over the fire plains of Mustafar that a Jedi Knight—a reputed protector of light, guardian of peace and life, and a hero of the Republic—had been spotted at the Mining Complex. The Mustafarian boy [Kakan](/wiki/Kakan "Kakan") hoped to exact his dream of meeting a Jedi, and so approached the fallen Anakin Skywalker.[[27]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Vader-27) The Sith Lord was viewing[[4]](#cite_note-ROTS-4) the eclipse of Mustafar's sun by Lefrani at the complex's balcony, just as Vader's massacre of the Separatists eclipsed the light of the Force within him.[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13)

However, Kakan saw that the figure was not the Jedi he expected. The fallen Jedi's eyes radiated such anger and hate that Kakan was compelled to run away, escaping to the complex's foundry. Kakan found the miner Lellis, who operated the facility's repulsor vents, releasing fumes from the depths of Mustafar that gave one illusions when inhaled. The potent fumes overwhelmed Vader with his fears, and Kakan and Lellis took advantage of his distraction to escape. However, as fear took hold of the boy as well, the two Mustafarians fell into a lava lake, but they were saved by a burst of Force energy released by Darth Vader in a bout of anger.[[27]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Vader-27)

##### To not let go[]

:   "*I hate you!*"
:   ―Darth Vader, to his former friend Obi-Wan Kenobi[[4]](#cite_note-ROTS-4)

 [![Battle of the heroes on Mustafar](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f8/DoctorAphra-30-HughesArt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190324051338) [![Battle of the heroes on Mustafar](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f8/DoctorAphra-30-HughesArt.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190324051338)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f8/DoctorAphra-30-HughesArt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190324051338) 

Battle of the heroes on Mustafar

 

Padmé Amidala had been rushing to Mustafar in the hope of saving her husband from falling further to the dark side. She arrived on the volcanic world shortly after the slaughter of the Separatist leaders, and Vader met her embrace at the Techno Union facility.[[12]](#cite_note-Mustafar_DB-12) Her pleas fell on deaf ears, however, when Vader spotted his former [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master"), [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"), emerging from Amidala's [ship](/wiki/J-type_Naboo_star_skiff "J-type Naboo star skiff"). In his anger, Vader incorrectly assumed that his lover had betrayed him for Kenobi and [strangled](/wiki/Force_choke "Force choke") her via the Force; Amidala thus realized that Anakin Skywalker had been consumed by his lust for power and was truly corrupted by the dark side.[[4]](#cite_note-ROTS-4)[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13)

Darth Vader then gave his old master and former friend an ultimatum: either he was with him or against him. Plagued by self-doubt and his inability to let go of his assumptions, Vader [attempted](/wiki/Duel_on_Mustafar "Duel on Mustafar") to slay Kenobi. As the two engaged in a [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel"), Vader bathed the remnants of his Jedi self in the dark side that echoed from Mustafar's Sith sanctum, and amid the chaos, the shields protecting the mining facility were shut down. Parts of the building as well as the *[Lapiz Cutter](/wiki/Lapiz_Cutter "Lapiz Cutter")*—the late Nute Gunray's personal [shuttle](/wiki/Sheathipede-class_transport_shuttle "Sheathipede-class transport shuttle")—were destroyed.[[60]](#cite_note-BMF54-60)

Forced to fight across the lava streams, Vader was fueled by hatred and, in his hubris, attacked without regard to his own limitations. He fell victim to Kenobi's [blade](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi%27s_third_lightsaber "Obi-Wan Kenobi's third lightsaber") beside a lava river. As the Sith Lord lost himself to the dark side's corruption, his remaining limbs were severed and his entire body was incinerated by Mustafar's lava.[[4]](#cite_note-ROTS-4)[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13)

##### Scarring legacies[]

:   "*Do not underestimate how much you disappointed me on Mustafar. I saved you—but you showed how far off the mark you fell…*"
:   ―Darth Sidious, to Darth Vader[[61]](#cite_note-DV6-61)

 [![Darth Sidious rescues his apprentice after he was left for dead on Mustafar's sands by Kenobi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f2/Let_The_Hate_Flow_AtG.png/revision/latest?cb=20191015013420) [![Darth Sidious rescues his apprentice after he was left for dead on Mustafar's sands by Kenobi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f2/Let_The_Hate_Flow_AtG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191015013420)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f2/Let_The_Hate_Flow_AtG.png/revision/latest?cb=20191015013420) 

Darth Sidious rescues his apprentice after he was left for dead on Mustafar's sands by Kenobi.

 

The fallen Jedi's [lightsaber](/wiki/Skywalker_lightsaber "Skywalker lightsaber") was then taken by Kenobi, who left him to die on the sands[[62]](#cite_note-ROTS_gallery-62) of the river bank. Kenobi then took Amidala to a [base](/wiki/Polis_Massa_Base "Polis Massa Base") on the [asteroid field](/wiki/Asteroid_field "Asteroid field") [Polis Massa](/wiki/Polis_Massa "Polis Massa") in order for her to give birth to her and Anakin Skywalker's children—the twins [Luke](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker") and [Leia](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"). Although charred and broken, Vader was recovered by Sidious, and he was brought back to Coruscant to be rebuilt with [cybernetics](/wiki/Cybernetics "Cybernetics") at[[4]](#cite_note-ROTS-4) the [Grand Republic Medical Facility](/wiki/Grand_Republic_Medical_Facility "Grand Republic Medical Facility")[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) with the technology of the acclaimed [scientist](/wiki/Scientist "Scientist") [Cylo](/wiki/Cylo "Cylo"),[[63]](#cite_note-DV20-63) becoming encased in a [suit](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_armor "Darth Vader's armor") of terrifying black [armor](/wiki/Armor "Armor").[[55]](#cite_note-USWNE-55)

Despite his survival, the events of Mustafar haunted Darth Vader throughout the age of the Empire, affecting the Sith's performance as the Emperor's[[63]](#cite_note-DV20-63)[[64]](#cite_note-Aphra_40-64) primary enforcer.[[65]](#cite_note-SithSWE-65) Seldomly, stories circulated amongst Mustafarians of a great Jedi duel on their world, although no evidence was given for such tales.[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24) Mustafarians nonetheless had knowledge of the former Jedi who slaughtered the Separatist leaders and nearly killed the boy Kakan and the miner Lellis, and whilst some thought that the fallen Jedi Knight was gone, others thought that he still remained in the mists of Mustafar. Years later, Lellis realized that Darth Vader was the very same fallen Jedi Knight, overshadowing his people since the rise of the Empire.[[27]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Vader-27)

Over a year after the battle against his former friend on Mustafar, in [18 BBY](/wiki/18_BBY "18 BBY"),[[66]](#cite_note-Ahsoka_date-66) the memory of Darth Vader burning on the volcanic slopes of Mustafar resurfaced in Obi-Wan Kenobi's thoughts along with other past happenings. Despite the pain inflicted by the memories, Kenobi willed himself to let go of his traumatic past and focus on his present—his mission to watch over Luke, the son of Anakin Skywalker.[[67]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-67)

### Vader's domain (19–9 BBY)[]

#### Sanctum of the Sith[]

:   "*When you arrive on Mustafar, find the place where the dark side calls to you. Draw upon the energy there—combine its power with your own. Then… use it.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious, to Darth Vader[[37]](#cite_note-DV5-37)

 [![Vader bled his new kyber crystal until it shone crimson.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/53/VaderBleeding-2017DarthVader5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170906135015) [![Vader bled his new kyber crystal until it shone crimson.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/53/VaderBleeding-2017DarthVader5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/320?cb=20170906135015)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/53/VaderBleeding-2017DarthVader5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170906135015) 

Vader bled his new kyber crystal until it shone crimson.

 

A short time after his loss to Kenobi, in 19 BBY,[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) Vader returned to Mustafar under instructions from Darth Sidious. Vader was to [bleed](/wiki/Bleeding "Bleeding") a kyber crystal he had obtained from the Jedi Master [Kirak Infil'a](/wiki/Kirak_Infil%27a "Kirak Infil'a"), who he killed, in order to gain a crimson [crystal](/wiki/Crystal "Crystal") for his new [Sith lightsaber](/wiki/Sith_lightsaber "Sith lightsaber"). He traveled to the dark side cave[[37]](#cite_note-DV5-37) that contained the shrine erected by the ancient Sith[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) and poured all of his pain and anger into the crystal, making it sing a hymn of darkness. With this new [weapon](/wiki/Kirak_Infil%27a%27s_lightsaber "Kirak Infil'a's lightsaber"), Vader returned to Coruscant by his master's side, another step closer, Sidious believed, to becoming a true servant of darkness.[[37]](#cite_note-DV5-37)

Although Sidious had lost his original facility during the Clone Wars,[[17]](#cite_note-Children_of_the_Force-17) he soon built additional installations on Mustafar where he continued to abduct Force-sensitive infants. Over time, he manipulated these children and molded them into new members of the [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius"),[[68]](#cite_note-BuildR2_33-68) a group of dark side [agents](/wiki/Jedi_hunter "Jedi hunter") trained by Darth Vader and initially made up of former Jedi, including [the Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/The_Grand_Inquisitor "The Grand Inquisitor"), since soon after the Empire's founding.[[69]](#cite_note-DV7-69)

In [14 BBY](/wiki/14_BBY "14 BBY"),[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) Vader captured the former Jedi [Chief Librarian](/wiki/Chief_Librarian "Chief Librarian") [Jocasta Nu](/wiki/Jocasta_Nu "Jocasta Nu"), a survivor of the [Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") at the end of the Clone Wars, and obtained a [memory crystal](/wiki/Memory_crystal "Memory crystal") given to Nu by [Jedi seekers](/wiki/Jedi_seeker "Jedi seeker") who identified potential [Jedi Initiates](/wiki/Jedi_Initiate "Jedi Initiate") from throughout the galaxy—it listed the names and locations of many Force-sensitives, including the individual [Nik Lowe](/wiki/Nik_Lowe "Nik Lowe") on Mustafar. Wary that the Emperor could replace him with another Force user, Vader murdered Nu and destroyed the memory crystal.[[70]](#cite_note-DV10-70)

After the [Chiss](/wiki/Chiss "Chiss") [Mitth'raw'nuruodo](/wiki/Mitth%27raw%27nuruodo "Mitth'raw'nuruodo") "Thrawn" came into contact with the Empire in 14 BBY,[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) having been attacked by a talented trio of [cadets](/wiki/Imperial_cadet "Imperial cadet") when he was studying at Coruscant's prestigious [Royal Imperial Academy](/wiki/Royal_Imperial_Academy "Royal Imperial Academy"), Thrawn recommended to [Commandant](/wiki/Commandant "Commandant") [Deenlark](/wiki/Deenlark "Deenlark") that his assailants be transferred away. When a derisive Deenlark asked if they should be transferred to Mustafar as punishment, Thrawn suggested that the three train instead as [starfighter](/wiki/Starfighter "Starfighter") [pilots](/wiki/Pilot "Pilot") at[[71]](#cite_note-Thrawn-71) the elite [Skystrike Academy](/wiki/Skystrike_Academy "Skystrike Academy") on the world [Montross](/wiki/Montross "Montross").[[72]](#cite_note-Skystrike_Academy-72)

#### Vader's plans[]

:   "*You created this design, in your last body. Tell me what it is.*"  
    "*The door to the dark side is locked. This is the key. Your beloved waits for you there, Vader. My fortress will tune the energies of the locus. It is your first step towards using the power of the dark side to pierce the veil of time, between life and death.*"
:   ―Darth Vader and Momin, on the design of Fortress Vader[[73]](#cite_note-DV22-73)

 [![Darth Vader wields his new crimson blade against Mustafarians, who were less than welcoming of their new neighbor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c0/MustafariansVsVader-2017DarthVader22.png/revision/latest?cb=20181201063717) [![Darth Vader wields his new crimson blade against Mustafarians, who were less than welcoming of their new neighbor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c0/MustafariansVsVader-2017DarthVader22.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/350?cb=20181201063717)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c0/MustafariansVsVader-2017DarthVader22.png/revision/latest?cb=20181201063717) 

Darth Vader wields his new crimson blade against Mustafarians, who were less than welcoming of their new neighbor.

 

Fascinated by the power he tapped into in the Sith cave on Mustafar,[[42]](#cite_note-DV21-42) and associating the world with his rebirth and personal connection to the dark side,[[55]](#cite_note-USWNE-55) Vader requested that the world be given to him by his master[[42]](#cite_note-DV21-42) in 14 BBY,[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) believing that the planet held the key to seeing the deceased Padmé Amidala once again. Gifted with the late Amidala's [royal starship](/wiki/Naboo_Royal_Starship "Naboo Royal Starship"), the [mask](/wiki/Mask_of_Lord_Momin "Mask of Lord Momin") of the ancient Sith heretic artisan [Darth Momin](/wiki/Darth_Momin "Darth Momin"), and a team of top Imperial [architects](/wiki/Architect "Architect"), Vader departed Coruscant for his new home. The Sith Lord entered the planet's violent atmosphere unshielded, causing severe damage to his vessel and casting a streak of fire across the smokey sky. His entry was witnessed by the Mustafarian [Father](/wiki/Father_(title) "Father (title)") [Kkkt](/wiki/Kkkt "Kkkt"), who warned his [clanmate](/wiki/Kkkt%27s_clan "Kkkt's clan") [Zzzs](/wiki/Zzzs "Zzzs") that the fireball was an omen of events to come.[[42]](#cite_note-DV21-42)

Landing near the Sith cave, Vader [meditated](/wiki/Meditation "Meditation") in its dark walls, leaving the Emperor's architects, [Colonel](/wiki/Colonel "Colonel") [Alva Brenne](/wiki/Alva_Brenne "Alva Brenne") and [Lieutenant](/wiki/Lieutenant "Lieutenant") [Roggo](/wiki/Roggo "Roggo"), to draw up plans for a personal base Vader could inhabit. Brenne [scouted](/wiki/Scout "Scout") the planet's terrain, believing that, although Vader was seemingly impossible to satisfy, she could manage to design a home suitable for the Dark Lord. Unbeknownst to the architects, the mask that Sidious had gifted Vader was [possessed](/wiki/Possession "Possession") by Darth Momin's spirit; it took control of Roggo, using his body to kill Brenne and create its own designs for the base.[[42]](#cite_note-DV21-42)

 [![Vader meditates in the Sith cave.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/VaderMeditatesInCave-2017DarthVader21.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200721212757) [![Vader meditates in the Sith cave.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/VaderMeditatesInCave-2017DarthVader21.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/350?cb=20200721212757)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/VaderMeditatesInCave-2017DarthVader21.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200721212757) 

Vader meditates in the Sith cave.

 

Vader confronted the spirit, killing its host body and demanding that it gives him answers. The spirit introduced itself as Momin and offered to help Vader construct a fortress that would harness the energies[[42]](#cite_note-DV21-42) of the dark side locus below the cave to open a door into the Force itself;[[55]](#cite_note-USWNE-55) through and beyond the limitations of [time](/wiki/Time "Time") and space.[[42]](#cite_note-DV21-42) Upon being [attacked](/wiki/Skirmish_on_Mustafar "Skirmish on Mustafar") by Father Kkkt's scout party, Vader abducted the Mustafarian [Sssp](/wiki/Sssp "Sssp") to serve as Momin's new body and let [Rrrn](/wiki/Rrrn "Rrrn") flee.
