The two Sith Lords subsequently took command of a vast Imperial construction force on the Gahenn Plains and began their work on what would become [Fortress Vader](/wiki/Fortress_Vader "Fortress Vader").[[73]](#cite_note-DV22-73)

Vader would exercise control over the entire Mustafar system.[[74]](#cite_note-Kenobi_IV-74) Around this time, the Inquisitorius' headquarters were moved from Coruscant to the moon [Nur](/wiki/Nur "Nur") in the Mustafar system, keeping close to Vader and his planet.[[75]](#cite_note-TSWB-75) A base[[74]](#cite_note-Kenobi_IV-74) but also a clandestine place of [incarceration](/wiki/Prison "Prison") and [torture](/wiki/Torture "Torture") for Jedi,[[76]](#cite_note-JFO-76) the [Fortress Inquisitorius](/wiki/Fortress_Inquisitorius "Fortress Inquisitorius") tower was built to complement the castle on Mustafar using black stone from the world[[77]](#cite_note-Dawn-77) in 14 BBY.[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43)

#### Portal to the past[]

:   "*I have been in contact with the other clanholds. We are not the only one affected—the entire planet screams at what the dark one is building on the Gahenn Plains.*"
:   ―Father Kkkt[[20]](#cite_note-DV23-20)

 [![Momin's imperfect designs caused chaos on Mustafar.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/FortressVaderLightning-2017DarthVader23.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200721230426) [![Momin's imperfect designs caused chaos on Mustafar.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/FortressVaderLightning-2017DarthVader23.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20200721230426)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/FortressVaderLightning-2017DarthVader23.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200721230426) 

Momin's imperfect designs caused chaos on Mustafar.

 

The construction of Vader's fortress was not a simple task. Over the course of eight attempts[[55]](#cite_note-USWNE-55) with at least five separate designs, Momin struggled to find the perfect structure that could correctly channel the dark side. The energy Vader exerted while attempting to open a rift in the locus caused electromagnetic storms to rage across the planet, throwing the world's creatures into a frenzy and casting the Mustafarian people into disarray—the natives found that their "lifefires" barely burned. As an [*Imperial*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Imperial-class_Star_Destroyer "Imperial-class Star Destroyer") loomed overhead, the new [Imperial garrison](/wiki/Fortress_Vader_Imperial_garrison "Fortress Vader Imperial garrison") managed to defend the site against small uprisings by the Mustafarians and lava fleas. Father Kkkt, realizing the danger Vader posed to his world, rallied the clanholds across Mustafar prepared to mount an [attack](/wiki/Battle_of_Fortress_Vader "Battle of Fortress Vader") on the Imperial intruders.[[20]](#cite_note-DV23-20)

Upon the completion of Momin's ninth design[[20]](#cite_note-DV23-20) in [12 BBY](/wiki/12_BBY "12 BBY"),[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) Vader was finally able to reach through the Force and open a [pathway into time](/wiki/Portal "Portal"), but he was interrupted in his moment of triumph by Kkkt and his forces. With the Dark Lord distracted, Momin entered the portal and claimed his original body, betraying Vader.[[20]](#cite_note-DV23-20) Kkkt's army had initial success in pushing back [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Junus](/wiki/Junus "Junus")' garrison, attacking the Imperials, whom they outnumbered by ten to one, with surprise tactics. Vader, however, soon arrived on the front lines and rallied his [magma troopers](/wiki/Magma_trooper "Magma trooper") to double their efforts. Recognizing Vader as the Imperial leader, Kkkt led the Mustafarians in a powerful [usage of the Force](/wiki/Telekinesis "Telekinesis"), drowning the enemy forces in a vast flood of lava. With his army wiped out, Vader retreated into the fortress, summoning his own massive force of energy to destroy the Mustafarian attackers.[[78]](#cite_note-DV24-78)

 [![Vader enters the portal in the Sith cave.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/SithCavePortal-2017DarthVader25.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181220013748) [![Vader enters the portal in the Sith cave.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/SithCavePortal-2017DarthVader25.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181220013748)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/SithCavePortal-2017DarthVader25.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181220013748) 

Vader enters the portal in the Sith cave.

 

Returning to the inner sanctum, Vader confronted Momin, who mocked the [cyborg](/wiki/Cyborg "Cyborg") Sith for his failures in service to the dark side. Using Momin's hubris against him, Vader crushed and killed the resurrected artist. With no one to stop him, he entered the portal,[[78]](#cite_note-DV24-78) encountering visions of his past and future, including his beloved wife, Padmé Amidala. Upon witnessing what her husband had become, however, the vision of Amidala ran from Vader, choosing to plunge into an abyss. A beam of light containing a figure that he did not know was his son then overwhelmed Vader.[[79]](#cite_note-DV25-79) Frustrated with the dark visions, Vader retreated and crushed the altar in the Sith cave, destroying the portal[[55]](#cite_note-USWNE-55) and accepting that the truth he encountered was exactly what he needed.[[79]](#cite_note-DV25-79) The Dark Lord later returned Momin's mask to Sidious;[[80]](#cite_note-Encyclopedia_Maul-80) both master and apprentice frequented Mustafar, using it to focus their meditation on the power of the dark side of the Force.[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13)

#### Mustafarian revolts[]

:   "*This is an* Imperial *facility.*"  
    "*And this is* our *world. A world with secrets that I have vowed to protect at all costs.*"
:   ―Rersey and Sssl[[25]](#cite_note-Return_5-25)

Black Sun departed Mustafar to a lower profile world after the Empire had established a garrison there.[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) The Techno Union similarly abandoned their operations, and their remaining resources were taken over by the Mining Guild, but they struggled to profit on Mustafar due to the strict travel restrictions imposed by the Empire.[[2]](#cite_note-Galactic_Explorer's_Guide-2) The Empire replenished their garrison[[30]](#cite_note-Tales_5-30) and maintained secret facilities on Mustafar where survivors of the Jedi Purge were interrogated and [executed](/wiki/Death_penalty "Death penalty"), although the lava planet remained publicly notable only for its mining operations.[[12]](#cite_note-Mustafar_DB-12) Rumor had it that Darth Vader carried out these interrogations, torturing the Jedi for any useful information before their execution.[[81]](#cite_note-Aftermath-81) As the world remained under heavy Imperial guard, mining operations there eventually ceased.[[82]](#cite_note-Tales_1-82)

In [11 BBY](/wiki/11_BBY "11 BBY"),[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) the term "[Mustafarian Special](/wiki/Mustafarian_Special "Mustafarian Special")" was used by [smuggler](/wiki/Smuggler "Smuggler") [Lando Calrissian](/wiki/Landonis_Balthazar_Calrissian "Landonis Balthazar Calrissian") and his [first mate](/wiki/First_Mate "First Mate"), [L3-37](/wiki/L3-37 "L3-37"), to refer to a [starfighter](/wiki/Starfighter "Starfighter") maneuver that involved great speed and surprise, and which ensured at least one side of a [starship confrontation](/wiki/Starfighter_combat "Starfighter combat") "end[ed] badly." L3-37 explained that the tactic was named such in reference to the eponymous lava world's fiery nature.[[33]](#cite_note-Lando's_Luck-33)

 [![According to a tale, an Imperial officer was driven insane by Mustafar's lava fumes and became Vader's servant Vaneé.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/VaneeMaster-ShadowOfVadersCastle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20201107093333) [![According to a tale, an Imperial officer was driven insane by Mustafar's lava fumes and became Vader's servant Vaneé.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/VaneeMaster-ShadowOfVadersCastle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/350?cb=20201107093333)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/VaneeMaster-ShadowOfVadersCastle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20201107093333) 

According to a tale, an Imperial officer was driven insane by Mustafar's lava fumes and became Vader's servant Vaneé.

 

Following Kkkt's failed attack and the completion of Fortress Vader[[30]](#cite_note-Tales_5-30)—according to a story told years later by the Mustafarian Lellis—Darth Vader sought candidates for a [servant](/wiki/Aide "Aide") who would attend to his needs, searching for [months](/wiki/Standard_month "Standard month") until a human named [Vaneé](/wiki/Vane%C3%A9 "Vaneé") came into his service[[27]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Vader-27) around 12 BBY.[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) During Vader's search, an [Imperial officer](/wiki/Imperial_officer "Imperial officer") was sent from [Imperial Command](/wiki/Imperial_High_Command "Imperial High Command") to Mustafar by [Moff](/wiki/Moff "Moff") [Seward](/wiki/Seward "Seward"), and was tasked with handling an outbreak of insanity amongst Imperial [lava troopers](/wiki/Volcanic_environment_stormtrooper "Volcanic environment stormtrooper") assigned to Fortress Vader. On Mustafar, the inspector found that the [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") had inhaled toxic fumes from the planet's depths that gave one illusions of fears and doubts, and he entered Vader's castle to speak with Darth Vader himself with the intention of resolving the matter. However, Vader, bathing in his [bacta tank](/wiki/Bacta_tank "Bacta tank"), instead forced the officer to inhale the fumes and confront his fears by holding him in place via the Force, refusing to let the human go. Face with the illusions caused by the Mustafarian fumes, the inspector denied their existence and began to laugh, laughing for days until he took advice from the voices by his head and became Vader's servant, named Vaneé.[[27]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Vader-27)

Eventually, years before the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor")[[27]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Vader-27) of [4 ABY](/wiki/4_ABY "4 ABY"),[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) the lava fumes leaking into Vader's castle were blocked off.[[27]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Vader-27) During the early days of Vader's reign over the planet, Vaneé witnessed the efforts of a second force of Mustafarians to push the Sith away from their homeworld. The group, led by [Criakan](/wiki/Criakan "Criakan"), desired vengeance for their slaughtered kin and [stormed](/wiki/Raid_on_Fortress_Vader "Raid on Fortress Vader") the fortress in a surprise attack. Surrounding Vaneé, Criakan and his forces intended to show no mercy to the Imperials, but were shown the same respect by Lord Vader, who cut them all down before they could burn down the castle.[[30]](#cite_note-Tales_5-30)

 [![Darth Vader fights Priestess Sssl's forces at Fortress Vader.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/ThirdAttackOnFortressVader-ReturnToVadersCastle5.png/revision/latest?cb=20200721064539) [![Darth Vader fights Priestess Sssl's forces at Fortress Vader.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/ThirdAttackOnFortressVader-ReturnToVadersCastle5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/350?cb=20200721064539)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/ThirdAttackOnFortressVader-ReturnToVadersCastle5.png/revision/latest?cb=20200721064539) 

Darth Vader fights Priestess Sssl's forces at Fortress Vader.

 

Sometime later, during a visit from the [Emperor's adviser](/wiki/Emperor%27s_adviser "Emperor's adviser") [Rersey](/wiki/Rersey "Rersey"), a third [attack on Fortress Vader](/wiki/Attack_on_Fortress_Vader "Attack on Fortress Vader") was undertaken by [Clan Rrrt](/wiki/Clan_Rrrt "Clan Rrrt")'s [Mother](/wiki/Mother_(title) "Mother (title)") [Sssl](/wiki/Sssl "Sssl"), a Mustafarian [priestess](/wiki/Priestess "Priestess") who could force her will upon others by subjecting them to a [mind-altering plague](/wiki/Unidentified_plague_(Mustafar) "Unidentified plague (Mustafar)"). Sssl's forces soon overwhelmed the Imperials, infecting Vader's soldiers and turning them against the Sith. Although Sssl had only intended to scare off the invaders, her plans changed when the Dark Lord himself was seemingly infected. In reality, Vader's mechanical body was immune to the plague, allowing him to feign subservience and draw the priestess out. Using a [mind trick](/wiki/Mind_trick "Mind trick"), Vader forced Sssl to order her own forces to drag her into the lava—a scene that made Rersey lose his sanity. Vaneé praised his master and noted that the Mustafarians would fear Vader's name in the future.[[25]](#cite_note-Return_5-25)

### Galactic war on Mustafar (9 BBY–1 ABY)[]

#### Rebels in peril[]

:   "*Yes the naval action at Mustafar was a short-term win. But the Empire now knows the measure of the Alliance's naval strength.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma, *The Rebel Files*[[83]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-83)

In [9 BBY](/wiki/9_BBY "9 BBY"),[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) Darth Vader conferred from Fortress Vader with the [Third Sister](/wiki/Reva_Sevander "Reva Sevander") via [hologram](/wiki/Hologram "Hologram") regarding their [hunt for Obi-Wan](/wiki/Hunt_for_Obi-Wan "Hunt for Obi-Wan") following a [failed attempt](/wiki/Search_for_Princess_Leia "Search for Princess Leia") to capture him.[[84]](#cite_note-Kenobi_III-84) Kenobi later [infiltrated](/wiki/Rescue_of_Princess_Leia_(9_BBY) "Rescue of Princess Leia (9 BBY)") Fortress Inquisitorius on the nearby moon Nur using intelligence from the [Hidden Path](/wiki/Hidden_Path "Hidden Path") rebels, who further found that Vader was not in the Mustafar system at the time, instead being aboard his [vessel](/wiki/Devastator "Devastator") elsewhere.[[74]](#cite_note-Kenobi_IV-74) The hunt was ultimately a failure, and from his castle, Vader was instructed by Darth Sidious via hologram to abandon his obsession with Kenobi.[[85]](#cite_note-Kenobi_VI-85)

 [![Imperial Star Destroyers stood watch over Mustafar.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/Imperial_Mustafar.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200415205927) [![Imperial Star Destroyers stood watch over Mustafar.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/Imperial_Mustafar.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/320?cb=20200415205927)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/Imperial_Mustafar.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200415205927) 

Imperial Star Destroyers stood watch over Mustafar.

 

In [4 BBY](/wiki/4_BBY "4 BBY"),[[48]](#cite_note-GA-48) the Jedi [Kanan Jarrus](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus") of the rebel cell named the [Spectres](/wiki/Spectres "Spectres") was detained aboard the [Imperial Star Destroyer](/wiki/Imperial_I-class_Star_Destroyer "Imperial I-class Star Destroyer") *[Sovereign](/wiki/Sovereign "Sovereign")*, the [flagship](/wiki/Flagship "Flagship") of [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin"), [Grand Moff](/wiki/Grand_Moff "Grand Moff")[[12]](#cite_note-Mustafar_DB-12) and [Governor](/wiki/Governor "Governor") of the Outer Rim.[[31]](#cite_note-AEYNK-31) The vessel entered Mustafar's orbit[[12]](#cite_note-Mustafar_DB-12) after the Empire's [capture](/wiki/Raid_on_the_communications_tower "Raid on the communications tower") of the Jedi on the Outer Rim planet [Lothal](/wiki/Lothal "Lothal"), where the Spectres were based.[[86]](#cite_note-Call_to_Action-86) Escorted by a [fleet](/wiki/Imperial_Navy "Imperial Navy") of three other [Star Destroyers](/wiki/Star_Destroyer "Star Destroyer") and support vessels, the *Sovereign* bore witness to the [Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/Grand_Inquisitor "Grand Inquisitor")'s interrogation of Jarrus for information about the rebellion and the informant named "[Fulcrum](/wiki/Fulcrum "Fulcrum")"[[12]](#cite_note-Mustafar_DB-12)—who was secretly the [former Jedi](/wiki/Force-Sensitive_Outcast "Force-Sensitive Outcast") Ahsoka Tano. [Hera Syndulla](/wiki/Hera_Syndulla "Hera Syndulla") led her Spectres crew on a [rescue mission](/wiki/Action_at_Mustafar "Action at Mustafar") over Mustafar. Using a stolen [Imperial Gozanti-class cruiser](/wiki/Evac_One "Evac One") and [TIE fighter](/wiki/Rebels_TIE_fighter "Rebels TIE fighter") to infiltrate the *Sovereign*, the Spectres freed their captive Jedi from the Grand Inquisitor. The latter's [lightsaber](/wiki/The_Grand_Inquisitor%27s_lightsaber "The Grand Inquisitor's lightsaber") was bisected during lightsaber combat against Jarrus and his Padawan, [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger"), and fell into the *Sovereign*'s [reactor](/wiki/Solar_ionization_reactor "Solar ionization reactor"), dooming the Star Destroyer. The Inquisitor himself chose to fall to his death rather than suffer for his failures.[[87]](#cite_note-Fire_Across_the_Galaxy-87)

With the aid of [Phoenix Cell](/wiki/Phoenix_Cell "Phoenix Cell"), a resistance group affiliated with "Fulcrum" in a growing network of rebels formed by Senators [Bail Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa") and [Mon Mothma](/wiki/Mon_Mothma "Mon Mothma"),[[83]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-83) the Spectres successfully fled the Mustafar system and joined the larger Phoenix Cell. Grand Moff Tarkin also evacuated from his flagship,[[87]](#cite_note-Fire_Across_the_Galaxy-87) which crashed into Mustafar's lava fields[[31]](#cite_note-AEYNK-31) in a defeat that embarrassed Tarkin and displeased Emperor Palpatine.[[88]](#cite_note-Epic_Battles-88) The skirmish over Mustafar marked one of the earliest rebel victories in the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War") against the Empire[[12]](#cite_note-Mustafar_DB-12) and heightened rebellious activity in the Outer Rim,[[89]](#cite_note-AlderaanCruiser-89) with unrest occuring on Lothal that [Imperial Security Bureau](/wiki/Imperial_Security_Bureau "Imperial Security Bureau") [Agent](/wiki/Agent "Agent") [Alexsandr Kallus](/wiki/Alexsandr_Kallus "Alexsandr Kallus") attributed to some [Lothalites](/wiki/Lothalite "Lothalite") perceiving the Empire as vulnerable following rumors of the Empire's show of weakness at Mustafar.[[87]](#cite_note-Fire_Across_the_Galaxy-87) Mon Mothma wrote in documents assembled in *[The Rebel Files](/wiki/The_Rebel_Files "The Rebel Files")* that the action at Mustafar was but a short-term success, considering that the rebels had revealed the naval capacity of their sector fleet to the Empire.[[83]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-83) Indeed, the Emperor sent Darth Vader to personally handle the rebel group.[[87]](#cite_note-Fire_Across_the_Galaxy-87)

Having become a part of Bail Organa's rebel network, Kanan Jarrus and Ezra Bridger began working with their fellow rebel Force-sensitive, Ahsoka Tano.[[87]](#cite_note-Fire_Across_the_Galaxy-87) In 3 BBY,[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) Tano reached out to Jarrus with report of her investigation on the Sith Lord who [attacked](/wiki/Siege_of_Lothal "Siege of Lothal") them over the planet [Lothal](/wiki/Lothal "Lothal") shortly prior—unbeknownst to them, he was Darth Vader[[90]](#cite_note-The_Future_of_the_Force-90) and formerly the Jedi Anakin Skywalker, who instructed Tano.[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) She had been monitoring transmissions from Mustafar, and while information on the Sith Lord remained elusive, she had gathered more intelligence on the Empire's Inquisitors. The former Jedi decoded two sets of coordinates from the Mustafar transmissions, and after she learned of an incident above the planet [Chandel](/wiki/Chandel "Chandel"), she and the Spectres investigated the world [Takobo](/wiki/Takobo "Takobo"), where they uncovered the Inquisitors' plot to kidnap Force-sensitive infants.[[90]](#cite_note-The_Future_of_the_Force-90) Tano recalled that it was similar to the kidnapping attempt that she and her master had foiled on Mustafar during the Clone Wars.[[17]](#cite_note-Children_of_the_Force-17)

In [1 BBY](/wiki/1_BBY "1 BBY"),[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) based on intelligence about the Empire's operations on Mustafar, a small [rebel](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") force was sent by Captain [Cassian Andor](/wiki/Cassian_Jeron_Andor "Cassian Jeron Andor") to infiltrate an [Imperial base](/wiki/Imperial_base_(Mustafar) "Imperial base (Mustafar)") located near Vader's castle and steal a vital artifact. Upon infiltrating the base, the rebels discovered the artifact was a [proto-saber](/wiki/Proto-saber "Proto-saber"), a precursor to the lightsaber, and escaped with information about the ancient weapon despite Vader's intervention.[[91]](#cite_note-Secrets-91)

#### Legacy of Corvax[]

:   "*Whoa. Whoa, that looks like—that looks like Mustafar. Mustafar's a mining planet. Why are the Imperials taking us there?*"
:   ―ZO-E3, to her captain[[14]](#cite_note-Immortal_1-14)

 [![A smuggler and ZO-E3 arrive at Mustafar.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/Windfall_above_Mustafar.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200118052013) [![A smuggler and ZO-E3 arrive at Mustafar.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/Windfall_above_Mustafar.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20200118052013)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/Windfall_above_Mustafar.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200118052013) 

A smuggler and ZO-E3 arrive at Mustafar.

 

In the same year,[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) while Mustafar maintained its reputation as a mining world, a [smuggler](/wiki/Corvax_descendant "Corvax descendant") and [ZO-E3](/wiki/ZO-E3 "ZO-E3") aboard the *[Windfall](/wiki/Windfall "Windfall")* were forcefully taken to Mustafar, having been taken out of [hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace") in the Mustafar system by an [*Interdictor*-class](/wiki/Interdictor-class_Star_Destroyer "Interdictor-class Star Destroyer") Star Destroyer commanded by [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") [Gable Karius](/wiki/Gable_Karius "Gable Karius").[[14]](#cite_note-Immortal_1-14) Karius served Vader as his second-in-command on Mustafar,[[92]](#cite_note-Karius-92) and the smuggler and ZO-E3 were held in Vader's castle. The Sith Lord then interrogated the smuggler, realizing that they had a strong connection to the Force and was a descendant of Lady Corvax. However, they then escaped below the castle to the underground Corvax Fortress, meeting the Mustafarian [Priestess](/wiki/Priestess_(Mustafarian) "Priestess (Mustafarian)") and activating [Lady Corvax's droid army](/wiki/Marching_Horde "Marching Horde") to [attack](/wiki/Battle_on_Mustafar "Battle on Mustafar") the Imperials.[[14]](#cite_note-Immortal_1-14)

Darth Vader briefly taught the Corvax descendant to harness the power of the Force in order to retrieve the Bright Star artifact, wishing to revive Padmé Amidala with it.[[22]](#cite_note-Immortal_2-22) The Sith Lord was prevented from doing so by the descendant, who staged an escape from the fortress and destroyed the Bright Star and the Aeon Engine, allowing Mustafar to begin restoring its forested ecosystems.[[38]](#cite_note-Immortal_3-38) Near Fortress Vader, the fertile soil grounds of[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) a bog named Corvax Fen began developing.[[54]](#cite_note-Inside_Intel-54)

#### Crushing aspirations[]

:   "*You seem unsettled.*"  
    "*No…just pressed for time.*"
:   ―Lord Vader and Director Krennic[[19]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-19)

 [![Orson Krennic arrives at Fortress Vader.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Vaders-shadow.png/revision/latest?cb=20200722065336) [![Orson Krennic arrives at Fortress Vader.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Vaders-shadow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20200722065336)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Vaders-shadow.png/revision/latest?cb=20200722065336) 

Orson Krennic arrives at Fortress Vader.

 

Later still in the year,[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) the Empire completed construction on the [Death Star](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station"), an orbital [battle station](/wiki/Battle_station "Battle station") capable of destroying a planet. After a [rebel attack](/wiki/Mission_to_Eadu "Mission to Eadu") on a [laboratory](/wiki/Eadu_Energy_Conversion_Laboratory "Eadu Energy Conversion Laboratory") on the world [Eadu](/wiki/Eadu "Eadu") threatened to expose the Death Star's capabilities to the galaxy at large,[[19]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-19) Vader summoned the [director](/wiki/Director "Director") of the project, [Orson Krennic](/wiki/Orson_Callan_Krennic "Orson Callan Krennic"), to his fortress on Mustafar.[[16]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_novel-16) Krennic, arriving while Vader was sustained within a [bacta](/wiki/Bacta "Bacta") tank,[[19]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-19) was escorted into Fortress Vader's rotunda by Vaneé to await the Dark Lord. Confronting the uneasy director, Vader admonished Krennic for his mistakes, using the Force to choke the aspirational officer when he further requested an audience with the Emperor. With his message relayed,[[16]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_novel-16) Vader watched Krennic's ship depart[[93]](#cite_note-RO_Adaptation_4-93) for the planet [Scarif](/wiki/Scarif "Scarif").[[16]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_novel-16) Despite Vader's threats, Krennic failed in his endeavors[[19]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-19) and the Death Star was soon destroyed by the Rebel Alliance. Around the same time, the rebels also destroyed the Empire's [Mirkanite Mining Facility](/wiki/Mirkanite_Mining_Facility "Mirkanite Mining Facility") on Mustafar.[[6]](#cite_note-BMF_17-6)

Later in the war, a [crew](/wiki/Lina_Graf%27s_crew "Lina Graf's crew") of rebels led by [Commander](/wiki/Commander "Commander") [Lina Graf](/wiki/Lina_Graf "Lina Graf") was [attacked](/wiki/Fact-finding_mission_to_the_Outer_Rim "Fact-finding mission to the Outer Rim") by Imperial forces, and their ship, the *[Auric](/wiki/Auric "Auric")*, was heavily damaged. They were forced to crash-land on Mustafar, a planet that Graf hoped would lead to her crew's salvation. Surrounded by lava, the rebels abandoned their ship and began toward the only structure in sight; Vader's fortress.[[82]](#cite_note-Tales_1-82)

They did not make it far before being attacked by Mustafar's exploding beetles. After defeating the beetles and arguing over the best course of action, Graf and her crew were cornered by a [squad](/wiki/Squad "Squad") of Imperial Lava Troopers.[[53]](#cite_note-Tales_2-53) Escaping the troopers, the group entered the fortress but soon became separated in its dark halls. Alerted to their presence by his aide Vaneé, Vader confronted the rebels,[[94]](#cite_note-Tales_4-94) capturing [Lieutenant](/wiki/Lieutenant "Lieutenant") [Thom Hudd](/wiki/Thom_Hudd "Thom Hudd")[[23]](#cite_note-Return_1-23) and destroying the [bodyguard droid](/wiki/Bodyguard_droid "Bodyguard droid") [XM-G3](/wiki/XM-G3 "XM-G3"),[[94]](#cite_note-Tales_4-94) although Graf and her remaining crew managed to escape Mustafar.[[30]](#cite_note-Tales_5-30) The rebels' successful escape from Vader's castle was remembered by the native Mustafarians by the aftermath of the Empire's collapse.[[27]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Vader-27)

 [![The Auric crashes on Mustafar.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/AuricCrashesOnMustafar-TalesFromVadersCastle1.png/revision/latest?cb=20200722061409) [![The Auric crashes on Mustafar.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/AuricCrashesOnMustafar-TalesFromVadersCastle1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200722061409)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/AuricCrashesOnMustafar-TalesFromVadersCastle1.png/revision/latest?cb=20200722061409) 

The *Auric* crashes on Mustafar.

 

For the next several [weeks](/wiki/Standard_week "Standard week"),[[95]](#cite_note-Return_4-95) Vaneé kept Hudd locked within the fortress and tortured him, all the while tormenting him with horrific tales from across the galaxy,[[96]](#cite_note-Return_3-96) including the story of Vader's brutal murder of Sssl years prior.[[25]](#cite_note-Return_5-25) The abuse and starvation that Hudd suffered while chained to the Sith servant's [torture web](/wiki/Torture_web "Torture web") was so severe that he lost enough body mass to slip from his shackles and escape his cell.[[96]](#cite_note-Return_3-96) Hudd managed to send a [distress signal](/wiki/Distress_signal "Distress signal") to the Alliance but was ultimately recaptured and sentenced to death. His execution was stalled by Graf, however, who had [returned](/wiki/Mission_to_Fortress_Vader "Mission to Fortress Vader") to Mustafar disguised as an [Inquisitor](/wiki/Fourth_Sister "Fourth Sister"). Although Vaneé saw through her ruse, Graf and Hudd were able to escape and flee the planet with the rest of their crew. Vader, angered at his servant's ineptitude, rigged Vaneé up to the torture web.[[25]](#cite_note-Return_5-25)

The loss of the Death Star served to galvanize resistance across the galaxy, causing trouble for the weakened Empire. In response to the outbreak of rebellion, Vader was met at Fortress Vader by Admiral [Kendal Ozzel](/wiki/Kendal_Ozzel "Kendal Ozzel") and [General](/wiki/General "General") [Maximilian Veers](/wiki/Maximilian_Veers "Maximilian Veers"). Overlooking Mustafar's lava fields, the trio discussed the proper route to deal with the rising Alliance, although Vader viewed Ozzel's suggestions as nothing more than excuses for incompetency. An interesting point from General Veers, however, persuaded Vader to view the rebels in a new light, prompting him to develop a different plan to [cripple](/wiki/Battle_of_Mako-Ta "Battle of Mako-Ta") the Alliance.[[97]](#cite_note-Shu-Torun_Lives-97)

### Crucible of fate and hate (3–4 ABY)[]

#### Into the fire[]

:   "*The last time you were* broken*…I* found *you…and I* rebuilt *you. This time… you must rebuild yourself.*"
:   ―Palpatine, to his battered apprentice[[98]](#cite_note-Vader_2020_6-98)

 [![Vader was mutilated and burned just as he was at the end of the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/HeBurnsAgain-2020DarthVader6.png/revision/latest?cb=20231113100140) [![Vader was mutilated and burned just as he was at the end of the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/HeBurnsAgain-2020DarthVader6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20231113100140)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/HeBurnsAgain-2020DarthVader6.png/revision/latest?cb=20231113100140) 

Vader was mutilated and burned just as he was at the end of the Clone Wars.

 

In [3 ABY](/wiki/3_ABY "3 ABY"),[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) Vader attempted to turn his son, Luke Skywalker, to the dark side during a [duel](/wiki/Duel_on_Cloud_City "Duel on Cloud City") over the planet [Bespin](/wiki/Bespin "Bespin"). After Skywalker [fled](/wiki/Escape_from_Cloud_City "Escape from Cloud City"), Vader temporarily abandoned his duties to the Emperor, embarking on a personal quest that led to the discovery of a [rebel cell](/wiki/Amidalans "Amidalans") led by [Sabé](/wiki/Sab%C3%A9 "Sabé"), the former [decoy](/wiki/Naboo_Royal_Handmaidens "Naboo Royal Handmaidens") of Padmé Amidala. Vader allowed the rebels to live, a decision which convinced Sidious that his apprentice was in need of a reminder of his place. The Emperor mutilated Vader on Coruscant, ripping his cybernetic limbs from his body and strangling him as he had done to men like Krennic in the past.[[98]](#cite_note-Vader_2020_6-98)

Not finished with his lesson, Sidious took his student back to Mustafar. He had Vader's [personal guard](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_guard "Darth Vader's guard") of [death troopers](/wiki/Death_trooper "Death trooper") drag him to the spot where Kenobi had defeated him decades ago, leaving the apprentice to fend for himself. Warned by his master that there would be consequences should he use the Force to save himself, a one-armed Vader crawled along the lava banks and retrieved his fallen lightsaber before slowly making his way to the ruins of the Techno Union installation. Sidious watched from Vader's [*Lambda*-class shuttle](/wiki/Lambda-class_T-4a_shuttle "Lambda-class T-4a shuttle") as the broken man pulled himself across the sand. Although [Mas Amedda](/wiki/Mas_Amedda "Mas Amedda"), the Emperor's [Grand Vizier](/wiki/Grand_Vizier "Grand Vizier"), warned that the Dark Lord planned to kill his master, Sidious was unconcerned and sent his [Sith assassin](/wiki/Sith_assassin "Sith assassin"), [Ochi of Bestoon](/wiki/Ochi "Ochi"), to turn Vader's anger into pain.[[98]](#cite_note-Vader_2020_6-98)

 [![Darth Vader meets with the Eye of Webbish Bog.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/58/VaderEyeOfWebbishBog-Revelations2022.png/revision/latest?cb=20250219200049) [![Darth Vader meets with the Eye of Webbish Bog.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/58/VaderEyeOfWebbishBog-Revelations2022.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/320?cb=20250219200049)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/58/VaderEyeOfWebbishBog-Revelations2022.png/revision/latest?cb=20250219200049) 

Darth Vader meets with the Eye of Webbish Bog.

 

Having reached the Techno Union installation ruins, the very building where he had slaughtered the Separatist Council decades prior, Vader repurposed surrounding Separatist droid parts as his own limbs and confronted Ochi, overpowering the assassin and demanding him to reveal Darth Sidious' plans. As Vader did so, the oracle [Eye of Webbish Bog](/wiki/Eye_of_Webbish_Bog "Eye of Webbish Bog") called out to the Sith Lord,[[99]](#cite_note-Vader_2020_7-99) who, despite being deprived of his chest box and [lightsaber](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_lightsaber "Darth Vader's lightsaber") by Ochi, fought his way through hordes of lava nymphs, lava fleas, and even a roggwart to reach the Eye's lava cavern. As Vader did so, he was tested by the Eye and reminded of his inner conflicts between his chosen Sith and Jedi destinies as well as between his personal desire of power and his need for his son. During Vader's journey to the Eye's lair, [Senior Administrative Aide](/wiki/Senior_Administrative_Aide "Senior Administrative Aide") [Sly Moore](/wiki/Sly_Moore "Sly Moore") and a group of death troopers spoke to Ochi, reminding the assassin to abide by the Emperor's directives.[[100]](#cite_note-Vader_2020_8-100)

At the end of Vader's trek to the Eye, the latter gave the cyborg a [wayfinder](/wiki/Vader%27s_wayfinder "Vader's wayfinder") and allowed him to leave the cavern to rejoin Ochi. Once outside, Vader made his way to the green Jedi starfighter that he took to Mustafar at the end of the Clone Wars,[[100]](#cite_note-Vader_2020_8-100) repairing the ship until Ochi reappeared with the [Droid Crush Pirates of Bestoon](/wiki/Droid_Crush_Pirates_of_Bestoon "Droid Crush Pirates of Bestoon"). Having been promised Vader's cybernetic parts by Ochi, the army of droid pursued the Emperor's enforcer until they found that his parts were no more special than their own. In the midst of a quarrel with Ochi about their deal, the droids were interrupted by Vader, who took down the machines for use in retrofitting his green starfighter and an [escape pod](/wiki/Escape_pod "Escape pod"), which he locked Ochi in after forcing the assassin to activate his wayfinder. In his determination to find the Emperor's secrets, Vader bound the pod to his starfighter and set off to the wayfinder's coordinates, reaching the [vicinity](/wiki/Red_Honeycomb_Zone "Red Honeycomb Zone") of the [Unknown Regions](/wiki/Unknown_Regions "Unknown Regions") world [Exegol](/wiki/Exegol "Exegol") via hyperspace.[[101]](#cite_note-Vader_2020_9-101)

 [![Darth Vader rebuilds his starfighter.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/ShipRepair-2020DarthVader9.png/revision/latest?cb=20240112010312) [![Darth Vader rebuilds his starfighter.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/ShipRepair-2020DarthVader9.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20240112010312)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/ShipRepair-2020DarthVader9.png/revision/latest?cb=20240112010312) 

Darth Vader rebuilds his starfighter.

 

With Ochi in tow, Vader confronted Sidious on Exegol, an ancient Sith world which housed hundreds of Sidious' secret experiments and weapons. The Emperor reminded his wayward apprentice that he left him weak and broken on Mustafar's burning shores, and asked Vader what he learned from the experience. However, Vader remained rebellious, stating his intention to make his "master" fear him. Despite Vader's efforts, he was overwhelmed by Sidious' power. Terribly pained, Vader, despite having experienced a vision of his son telling him it was his destiny to destroy Sidious, accepted his master's dominance over him before leaving Exegol with him and Ochi.[[102]](#cite_note-Vader_2020_11-102)

#### Crimson Dawn intrusion[]

:   "Ha! *You lose,* chump!"  
    "Uh, *boss, you sure that's such a good idea?*"
:   ―Ren, shouting at Vader, and a Knight of Ren[[45]](#cite_note-CR_4-45)

Later, between 3 ABY and 4 ABY,[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) Lady [Qi'ra](/wiki/Qi%27ra "Qi'ra")'s criminal syndicate, [Crimson Dawn](/wiki/Crimson_Dawn "Crimson Dawn"), hired the [Knights of Ren](/wiki/Knights_of_Ren "Knights of Ren"), a group of dark side warriors, to [raid](/wiki/Heist_on_Vader%27s_Castle "Heist on Vader's Castle") Fortress Vader and acquire the [Screaming Key](/wiki/Screaming_Key "Screaming Key") artifact[[45]](#cite_note-CR_4-45)—Darth Sidious had placed the key there, but did not know that it unlocked Momin's fabled [Fermata Cage](/wiki/Fermata_Cage "Fermata Cage"), which held power that threatened even the Sith.[[103]](#cite_note-HE_1-103) In her [quest](/wiki/War_against_the_Sith "War against the Sith") to destroy the Sith, Qi'ra had obtained the full layout,[[45]](#cite_note-CR_4-45) access codes,[[104]](#cite_note-CR_1-104) and security details of the fortress and convinced the Knights' [leader](/wiki/Ren "Ren"), [Ren](/wiki/Ren_(human) "Ren (human)"), to go ahead with the raid despite initial reluctance from other Knights. The Knight [Massif](/wiki/Massif "Massif") had complained that "the job was too hot" not just because Mustafar's surface was a hellscape, and fellow Knights [Bazzra](/wiki/Bazzra "Bazzra") and [Marinda](/wiki/Marinda "Marinda") also had their own concerns. Nevertheless, Qi'ra promised the Knights glory and the freedom to claim any objects to keep for themselves aside from the key.[[45]](#cite_note-CR_4-45)

 [![The Knights of Ren enter Fortress Vader through the Sith cave.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/78/KnightsOfRenSithCave-CrimsonReign4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220428044754) [![The Knights of Ren enter Fortress Vader through the Sith cave.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/78/KnightsOfRenSithCave-CrimsonReign4.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/290?cb=20220428044754)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/78/KnightsOfRenSithCave-CrimsonReign4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220428044754) 

The Knights of Ren enter Fortress Vader through the Sith cave.

 

The group landed their [vessel](/wiki/Oubliette-class_transport "Oubliette-class transport"), the *[Night Buzzard](/wiki/Night_Buzzard "Night Buzzard")*, on the Gahenn Plains and used [speeder bikes](/wiki/Speeder_bike "Speeder bike") to approach the fortress from the south. Ren had concluded that the sensors of the Imperial garrison on the building's far side could not detect them given Mustafar's magnetic field, and as they used their speeder's signal [jammers](/wiki/Jammer "Jammer"), they were able to approach undetected. The Knights approached an old entrance to the fortress that was covered by lava, but by using the Force to clear a way through, they entered the Sith cave below the installation. The helmet of Momin still lay in the cave, which spooked Bazzra into shooting and destroying it. They then continued on their route towards the vault.[[45]](#cite_note-CR_4-45)

 [![Ren duels Darth Vader.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/RenVaderDuel-CrimsonReign4.png/revision/latest?cb=20230715121557) [![Ren duels Darth Vader.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/RenVaderDuel-CrimsonReign4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20230715121557)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/RenVaderDuel-CrimsonReign4.png/revision/latest?cb=20230715121557) 

Ren duels Darth Vader.

 

As they neared the vault, the Knights were spotted by Vaneé, who warned them that it was too late for them to turn back and that Vader would learn of their presence. The Knights turned their weapons on Vaneé, but he was protected by a force field. Meanwhile, a large group of lava troopers surrounded the Knights and a battle began. As the Knights fought their way to the vault, Ren began to cut open the door to the vault with [his lightsaber](/wiki/Ren_(lightsaber) "Ren (lightsaber)"). Inside the vault, Ren used the Force to listen for the Screaming Key, and located the small gray key. Realizing that the battle had also gone quiet, Ren asked if they had defeated all the troopers, and while the Knights told him that they had all departed for unexplained reasons, Darth Vader emerged. Vader quickly killed the Knight [Fyodor](/wiki/Fyodor "Fyodor") with a Force choke before Ren engaged him in lightsaber combat. As Vader and Ren traded blows, Vader learned that his opponents were the Knights of Ren. The remaining Knights fled at Ren's command, and Ren soon jumped out of a window to join them, using [controlled descent](/wiki/Controlled_descent "Controlled descent") to survive the fall. Vader attempted to use the Force to grab the key back out of Ren's hand, but the other Knights fired their blasters at Vader, forcing him to use his energy to deflect their shots. The Knights then fled on their speeders and left Mustafar with the key, which they delivered to Qi'ra's ally, [The Archivist](/wiki/The_Archivist "The Archivist"), at a [location](/wiki/Dark_side_hellscape "Dark side hellscape") where The Archivist believed the Fermata Cage to be.[[45]](#cite_note-CR_4-45)

#### Scourge and Schism[]

:   "*I have never been* stronger*.*"
:   ―Darth Vader, training to focus his abilities on Mustafar[[105]](#cite_note-DV202037-105)

The Eye of Webbish Bog called out to Vader, who entered his lair and experienced visions that the being hoped would serve as a warning to the Sith Lord of an impending culmination of interconnected galactic events. After receiving the visions, Vader found that the Eye was being poisoned by a device left in his cave and subsequently ambushed by several Mustafarians. The natives were unhappy with the Sith Lord's intrusion on their planet, but Vader dispatched them at the cost of only a scar left on his helmet and eliminated the device that had been plaguing the Eye. The Sith then returned to his castle, where he spoke with the Emperor via hologram about Lady Qi'ra's machinations against them.[[106]](#cite_note-Revelations-106)

After the Sith overcame Qi'ra's [attempt](/wiki/Battle_at_Amaxine_Station "Battle at Amaxine Station") to defeat them, Luke Skywalker communicated with a red kyber crystal on the planet [Christophsis](/wiki/Christophsis "Christophsis"), in the process experiencing a vision in which he saw Fortress Vader in the midst of a red lightning storm as well as his father, Darth Vader.[[107]](#cite_note-2020SW35-107) Qi'ra's activation of the Fermata Cage during her war against the Sith had [destabilized](/wiki/Force_Wave "Force Wave") Vader's mastery of the Force, and the Dark Lord, wielding the [Zaly Shield](/wiki/Zaly_Shield "Zaly Shield") alongside a [staff](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_electrostaff "Darth Vader's electrostaff"), returned to the lava fields before his castle to train himself in focusing his powers.[[105]](#cite_note-DV202037-105) Meanwhile, the [Scourge](/wiki/Scourge "Scourge"), a droid-possessing [malady](/wiki/Scourge_crisis "Scourge crisis"), intended to control Vader as he was a cyborg who could use the Force. It arrived on Mustafar as the corrupted rebel [protocol droid](/wiki/3PO-series_protocol_droid "3PO-series protocol droid") [C-3PO](/wiki/C-3PO "C-3PO") and as the [MSE-6 droid](/wiki/MSE-6_series_repair_droid "MSE-6 series repair droid") [Petyr](/wiki/Petyr "Petyr") on a [Taylander shuttle](/wiki/Taylander_shuttle "Taylander shuttle").[[108]](#cite_note-Dark_Droids_2-108) The initial [attack on Fortress Vader](/wiki/Scourge_attack_on_Fortress_Vader "Scourge attack on Fortress Vader") failed as the Scourge's attention was diverted by an [attack](/wiki/Attack_on_Scourge_01 "Attack on Scourge 01") elsewhere and the breakthrough of being able to control the consciousness of cyborg organics.[[109]](#cite_note-Dark_Droids_3-109)

While training with his droid army, Vader received a hologram transmission from Grand Vizier Amedda, who relayed the Emperor's order to reclaim his flagship, the *[Executor](/wiki/Executor "Executor")*—it had been [infiltrated](/wiki/Attack_on_the_Executor_(Scourge_crisis) "Attack on the Executor (Scourge crisis)") by the Scourge. Vader and his droids thus departed for the *Executor* aboard an [Imperial transport](/wiki/Imperial_Troop_Transport "Imperial Troop Transport").[[105]](#cite_note-DV202037-105) After successfully reclaiming the flagship, the Sith Lord took his droids and his personal [TIE fighter](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_TIE_Advanced "Darth Vader's TIE Advanced") and returned to Mustafar, where another droid repaired its fellow veterans while Vader confronted the Eye of Webbish Bog, demanding power and control—while battling the Scourge, Amedda had ordered the *Executor*'s destruction with Vader onboard. The Eye reminded Vader that power lied with his master, Darth Sidious, citing the [Tragedy of Darth Plagueis the Wise](/wiki/Tragedy_of_Darth_Plagueis_the_Wise "Tragedy of Darth Plagueis the Wise") in which Sidious murdered his own master. While Vader prepared to depart for Coruscant's Imperial Palace with his droids and a *Lambda*-class [shuttle](/wiki/Shuttle "Shuttle"), one of his droids, [ZED-6-7](/wiki/ZED-6-7 "ZED-6-7"), succumbed to the Scourge and activated an [octuptarra tri-droid](/wiki/Octuptarra_tri-droid "Octuptarra tri-droid") in the secret Techno Union droid factory.[[110]](#cite_note-DV202038-110)

The octuptarra [attacked](/wiki/Attack_on_Vader "Attack on Vader") Vader on the lava plains, and the Sith Lord's crude Force power through his Zaly Shield and staff proved ineffective. In their attempt to trigger Vader's hatred so that he could further draw on the dark power that hate channeled, the Dark Lord's droids [Gee-Ninety](/wiki/G-90 "G-90") and [Arex](/wiki/Arex "Arex") joined in the attack, but to no avail. Arex urged the Sith to think about what he hated most, and the cyborg realized that he hated himself; using his self-loathing, Vader channeled his hate into fine Force power to destroy the Scourge's octuptarra, damaging Gee-Ninety, Arex, and ZED-6-7 in the process. Vader also found that he hated his master, Darth Sidious, even more than himself, and set off for Coruscant[[111]](#cite_note-DV202039-111) with a compliment of Scourge [spider-droids](/wiki/Spider-droid "Spider-droid") aboard his [TIE Advanced x1](/wiki/TIE_Advanced_x1 "TIE Advanced x1"), setting the stage for a confrontation with his master and the [Scourge of Coruscant](/wiki/Scourge_of_Coruscant "Scourge of Coruscant").[[112]](#cite_note-DV202040-112)

Vader's attack failed, as the Emperor turned Vader's own troops, including his hand-picked squad of death troopers, against him.[[112]](#cite_note-DV202040-112) Vader eliminated the squad and had their bodies sent to a medical lab on Mustafar. There the Sith Lord mused that although the death troopers organic minds made them superior to droids, it also supplied them with a will that could be turned against him.[[113]](#cite_note-Tool_of_the_Empire-113) Following the end of the droid crisis, Vader sought to appropriate the Scourge's ability to control automatons and cyborgs for his own ends. The Dark Lord captured the members of [M.A.R. Corps](/wiki/M.A.R._Corps "M.A.R. Corps")—a Rebel Alliance squad of cybernetically-enhanced commandos—and brought them to Mustafar for experimentation. Under the supervision of ZED-6-7, the rebels were equipped with droid brains that allowed Vader to interface with and command them. The process was extremely invasive, however, causing severe mental anguish in the commandos that was shared by Vader. During these experiments, [Administrator](/wiki/Administrator "Administrator") Sly Moore met with Vader in his fortress with the intent of persuading him to join her [Schism Imperial](/wiki/Schism_Imperial "Schism Imperial"), a splinter group of disaffected Imperial officers and bureaucrats who planned to overthrow the Emperor.[[114]](#cite_note-DV202042-114)

Vader and the Schism's crusade against the Emperor finally came to a head in a skirmish on [Caranthanax B](/wiki/Caranthanax_B "Caranthanax B"), where Vader fully submitted to the will of the Emperor. The aftermath of the battle saw the Schism revealed as a ruse concocted by Palpatine, as well the recovery of [energy capsules](/wiki/Energy_capsule_(technology) "Energy capsule (technology)") from the site by the former slaves [Kitster Banai](/wiki/Kitster_Banai "Kitster Banai") and [Wald](/wiki/Wald "Wald"). Ochi of Bestoon later recovered the capsules on [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine") and presented them to Vader in his castle throne room on Mustafar.[[115]](#cite_note-DV202050-115)

### Ashes of Empire (4–35 ABY)[]

#### Lingering darkness[]

:   "*It is not over. Not yet. Not while you can bring him back…your master will* return *to the fires of Mustafar and, this time, will be made whole… Vader triumphant. Vader supreme. Vader…* reborn*!*"
:   ―A voice speaks to Vaneé[[27]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Vader-27)

Toward the end of the Galactic Civil War, Vader was saved by the selfless compassion of his son, Luke Skywalker, and in turn sacrificed himself to destroy the Emperor[[116]](#cite_note-Anakin_DB-116) aboard the [second Death Star](/wiki/DS-2_Death_Star_II_Mobile_Battle_Station "DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station") during the Battle of [Endor](/wiki/Endor "Endor") in 4 ABY.[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) Having re-embraced his identity as Anakin Skywalker as he succumbed to the injuries [inflicted](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning") upon him by his late Sith Master,[[117]](#cite_note-ROTJ-117) Vader died leaving his fortress without a host.[[27]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Vader-27) After the battle, [pilot](/wiki/New_Republic_pilot "New Republic pilot") [Wedge Antilles](/wiki/Wedge_Antilles "Wedge Antilles") scouted suspected Imperial planets and reported his findings to the leadership of the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic")—the Rebellion's successor state—on the world [Raydonia](/wiki/Raydonia "Raydonia"); due to Mustafar's proximity to Raydonia, Admiral [Gial Ackbar](/wiki/Gial_Ackbar "Gial Ackbar") sent a scout to there, along with the planets Tatooine, [Dermos](/wiki/Dermos "Dermos"), [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis"), and [Akiva](/wiki/Akiva "Akiva").[[81]](#cite_note-Aftermath-81)

Following news of Darth Vader's death over Endor that the Rebel Alliance had broadcasted, Mustafarians gathered around the fortress' vicinity in celebration. Lightning storm clouds and lava on Mustafar stirred around Vader's castle, howls sounded in the night, and cries echoed across the lava plains. The Mustafarian boy [Giggek](/wiki/Giggek "Giggek") recognized that his kind were not truly free as long as they lived under the shadow of Vader's castle, and so resolved to rid the land of Vader's curse by bringing the castle to ruin. Along with [Tuttel](/wiki/Tuttel "Tuttel"), Giggek acquired [detonators](/wiki/Bomb "Bomb") from a store of equipment from the obsidian mines belonging to Tuttel's uncle, Lellis. However, the latter forbid the young boys from entering Vader's castle for the reason that it was lethal and evil, telling the story of how Vaneé came into servitude under Vader and further speculating that the young Mustafarians were only pursuing glory.[[27]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Vader-27)

 [![Two young Mustafarians ventured into Fortress Vader despite being cautioned against doing so by Lellis.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/LellisWarnsGiggek-ShadowOfVadersCastle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20201107110104) [![Two young Mustafarians ventured into Fortress Vader despite being cautioned against doing so by Lellis.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/LellisWarnsGiggek-ShadowOfVadersCastle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/360?cb=20201107110104)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/LellisWarnsGiggek-ShadowOfVadersCastle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20201107110104) 

Two young Mustafarians ventured into Fortress Vader despite being cautioned against doing so by Lellis.

 

Nevertheless, Giggek led Tuttel into Vader's castle by way of lava flea, venturing in to find a pit trapping Vaneé, the servant of Vader and the self-styled "one true [Acolyte of the Beyond](/wiki/Acolytes_of_the_Beyond "Acolytes of the Beyond")" who was detained by Vader there some time ago. Rescuing the Acolyte in hopes of not bringing death upon anyone in the process of destroying Vader's castle, Giggek was at once betrayed by Vaneé, who dropped the boy down the pit in hopes of bringing death to those who sought to tarnish his master's legacy. However, after instructing his Mustafarian companion to flee, which Tuttel did with their lava flea, Giggek ignited his explosives through a remote [detonator](/wiki/Detonator "Detonator"), and although the blast did not bring down Vader's castle, Vaneé was buried in black sand. However, the Sith servant survived. A voice familiar to Vaneé told him not to fear, and assured its servant that he could return Vader to the fires of Mustafar and be made whole.[[27]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Vader-27)

#### Wrath of Vader's ghost[]

:   "*And I'm sorry. You of all people must be—*"  
    "*Scared out of my wits? Wishing I'd never even heard the* word *Mustafar? It's the dreams, Lina. They're getting to us all.*"  
    "*You're right, Hudd. That's all they are… dreams. And dreams aren't real… Dreams can't hurt you.*"
:   ―Lina Graf and Thom Hudd, on Mustafar once more[[118]](#cite_note-Ghosts_4-118)

At some point, Vaneé witnessed holonews reports on the Battle of Endor and the death of Vader, but he refused to believe that his master had met his end. The acolyte continued to maintain the Dark Lord's castle, anticipating his return at any time.[[119]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vaneé-119) Following the Empire's defeat at[[120]](#cite_note-Ghosts_1-120) the [Battle of Jakku](/wiki/Battle_of_Jakku "Battle of Jakku") in [5 ABY](/wiki/5_ABY "5 ABY"),[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) Vaneé told the voice he believed to be his master that everyone in the galaxy believed that he was dead, which the supposed ghost of Vader replied to by saying that the Sith can never truly be killed since it was the will of the dark side. Vaneé then orchestrated a ritual in which Vader's ghost reached out across the galaxy to imprint nightmares upon others' minds. One such nightmare reached [Milo Graf](/wiki/Milo_Graf "Milo Graf"), brother of Lina Graf, in which Milo had a nightmare about undead droids and himself being taken to Mustafar by [CR-8R](/wiki/CR-8R "CR-8R"), controlled by Vaneé.[[120]](#cite_note-Ghosts_1-120)

After he discussed Vader's castle with his sister and CR-8R, Milo Graf and the droid went missing for days[[121]](#cite_note-Ghosts_2-121)—CR-8R had been afflicted by a signal that scrambled his processors[[122]](#cite_note-Ghosts_5-122) and had incapacitated the organic before bringing him to Vaneé on Mustafar. Suffering from a dream of her brother being trapped on Mustafar, Lina requested New Republic [Chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor_(New_Republic) "Chancellor (New Republic)") Mon Mothma and Senator [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") on the capital world [Chandrila](/wiki/Chandrila "Chandrila") to spare a ship to investigate the lava world, which had remained under Imperial control. Although Mothma denied Graf's request, Organa suggested that she contact the smuggler [Jaxxon T. Tumperakki](/wiki/Jaxxon_T._Tumperakki "Jaxxon T. Tumperakki") for passage to Mustafar.[[121]](#cite_note-Ghosts_2-121) Before arriving at Vader's castle, they enlisted Graf's old crew, Thom Hudd and [Skritt](/wiki/Skritt "Skritt"); Hudd had also been experiencing nightmares related to Vaneé and the fortress.[[123]](#cite_note-Ghosts_3-123)

En route to Mustafar aboard the *[Rabbit's Foot](/wiki/Rabbit%27s_Foot "Rabbit's Foot")*, Lina Graf experienced a nightmare where her crew was attacked by an Imperial [*Gozanti*-class cruiser](/wiki/Gozanti-class_Assault_Carrier "Gozanti-class Assault Carrier") and TIE fighters upon arriving in the Mustafar system. Mid-battle, Lina Graf was attacked by the phantom of Darth Vader and encountered her brother, Milo, who transformed into Darth Vader and killed her crewmates. When Lina awoke from her nightmare, her crew and their ship had landed at Fortress Vader.[[118]](#cite_note-Ghosts_4-118) While the crew broke into the installation, Lina was contacted by Milo via comlink, pleading to be rescued. They then encountered a machine resembling Darth Vader and wielding a blue-bladed lightsaber, but promptly destroyed it and found CR-8R, who regained his normal processing and revealed Vaneé to be the mastermind.[[122]](#cite_note-Ghosts_5-122)

 [![Anakin Skywalker as a Force spirit, having rescued the crew of Lina Graf from the ghosts of Vader's castle](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5b/AnakinGhost-GhostsOfVadersCastle5.png/revision/latest?cb=20211025001242) [![Anakin Skywalker as a Force spirit, having rescued the crew of Lina Graf from the ghosts of Vader's castle](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5b/AnakinGhost-GhostsOfVadersCastle5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20211025001242)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5b/AnakinGhost-GhostsOfVadersCastle5.png/revision/latest?cb=20211025001242) 

Anakin Skywalker as a Force spirit, having rescued the crew of Lina Graf from the ghosts of Vader's castle

 

Vaneé soon captured the crew, intending to use them for a ritual that supposedly would revive Darth Vader. He released lava fumes into the captivity chamber, declaring that Lina Graf would be the vessel for Vader's return and that the Dark Lord would be immortal, ushering a new empire. However, Lina saw through Vaneé's madness and the hallucinations brought by the lava fumes, conquering her fear; taking advantage of Vaneé's fear for Vader, she deceived the man and freed her crew with the blue lightsaber. Upon forcing Vaneé into the restraints that he had used to detain her, Lina fled just as her blade extinguished, leaving Vaneé trapped with his own nightmares within the castle. Before departing Mustafar safely, however, Lina's crew followed the light of a blue blade in order to flee Fortress Vader—unbeknownst to them, the light was created by the [Force spirit](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit") of Anakin Skywalker, Jedi Knight.[[122]](#cite_note-Ghosts_5-122)

#### A healing world[]

:   "*Black Sun is currently headquartered on the lava planet Mustafar and is mainly controlled by Vigos from several noble Falleen families.*"
:   ―"Index of Organizations"[[124]](#cite_note-Species_From_A_to_Z-124)

 [![Vader's Castle battlefield on Vespaara](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/VadersCastleBattlefield-SWH.png/revision/latest?cb=20250326161430) [![Vader's Castle battlefield on Vespaara](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/VadersCastleBattlefield-SWH.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20250326161430)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/VadersCastleBattlefield-SWH.png/revision/latest?cb=20250326161430) 

Vader's Castle battlefield on Vespaara

 

Mustafar grew in obscurity in the decades that followed, and Vader's castle eventually fell into ruins.[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) Thanks to the destruction of the Bright Star,[[38]](#cite_note-Immortal_3-38) Mustafar's ecosystem began to be healed.[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) In [9 ABY](/wiki/9_ABY "9 ABY"),[[125]](#cite_note-Hunters_Date-125) the competitive sporting show [Hunters of the Outer Rim](/wiki/Hunters_of_the_Outer_Rim "Hunters of the Outer Rim") featured many battlefields for the [Hunters](/wiki/Hunter_(Grand_Arena) "Hunter (Grand Arena)") to compete in, including [Vader's Castle](/wiki/Vader%27s_Castle "Vader's Castle")—a battlefield that was designed after Fortress Vader and Mustafar's scorching environment—at the [Grand Arena](/wiki/Grand_Arena "Grand Arena") on the planet [Vespaara](/wiki/Vespaara "Vespaara"). To complete the immersion of the battlefield, a wide screen projection was used at the side to display Mustafar's rocky terrain and flowing lava rivers.[[126]](#cite_note-SWH-126) One Hunter, the former stormtrooper [Sentinel](/wiki/Sentinel "Sentinel"), claimed to have been deployed to a very hot lava planet and claimed to have fought a [Fireworm](/wiki/Fireworm "Fireworm") on that world, although he could not recall if it had been Mustafar or [Senna](/wiki/Senna "Senna"). However, another Hunter, [Imara Vex](/wiki/Imara_Vex "Imara Vex"), was quick to warn fans that Sentinel could not always be taken at his word.[[127]](#cite_note-Sentinel_M2-127)

Around the same year,[[128]](#cite_note-Skeleton_Crew_Date-128) the [astronomer](/wiki/Astronomer "Astronomer") [Kh'ymm](/wiki/Kh%27ymm "Kh'ymm") attempted to uncover the coordinates to the long-lost planet [At Attin](/wiki/At_Attin "At Attin") from her [facility](/wiki/Unidentified_telescopic_array "Unidentified telescopic array") on the [Observatory Moon](/wiki/Observatory_Moon "Observatory Moon"). Mustafar was one of the many worlds in her database that she scoured through to find the legendary planet.[[129]](#cite_note-Astrogation_Problem-129) A variety of individuals from off-world visited the planet during this period,[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) including the spy [Vi Moradi](/wiki/Vi_Moradi "Vi Moradi")[[130]](#cite_note-Return_to_a_Shattered_Planet-130) as well as the [historian](/wiki/Historian "Historian") and adventurer [Eloc Throno](/wiki/Eloc_Throno "Eloc Throno"), who wrote of the world in *[Volcanic Planets: Your Guide to the Galaxy's Hottest Destinations](/wiki/Volcanic_Planets:_Your_Guide_to_the_Galaxy%27s_Hottest_Destinations "Volcanic Planets: Your Guide to the Galaxy's Hottest Destinations")*, one of the many travel guides he wrote throughout his career.[[131]](#cite_note-Travel_Guide_to_Batuu-131) By the [New Republic Era](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era"), Black Sun had resumed operations on Mustafar, which served as its headquarters. During this time, Mustafar was also mentioned in "[Index of Organizations](/wiki/Index_of_Organizations "Index of Organizations")," a survival compendium sent out by [Carson Teva](/wiki/Carson_Teva "Carson Teva"), which mentioned Black Sun's operations as well as the rescue of Marg Krim's family during the Clone Wars.[[124]](#cite_note-Species_From_A_to_Z-124)

By [34 ABY](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY"),[[132]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_Date-132) many pilgrims had come to the ruins of Vader's castle seeking to tap into the Sith Lord's dark power. One group of pilgrims,[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) the [Alazmec of Winsit](/wiki/Alazmec_of_Winsit "Alazmec of Winsit"), guarded the castle ruins as well as its secrets jealously,[[12]](#cite_note-Mustafar_DB-12) colonizing the nearby Corvax Fen and planting a forest of irontrees in the hopes of restoring Mustafar's once lush landscape from centuries ago, believing that the soil was soaked by the tears of Lady Corvax.[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) The [cultists](/wiki/Sith_cultist "Sith cultist") cared for the trees as they sought to connect to the power of the Sith.[[133]](#cite_note-CEUEE-133) The Alazmec also venerated Vader's memory and defended Mustafar's secrets against seekers whom they considered unworthy.[[134]](#cite_note-Alazmec_DB-134) Vader's aging advisor Vaneé lived amongst them at the Dark Lord's castle;[[135]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-135) though ancient by human standards, he had extended his lifespan through extreme cybernetic augmentations not unlike those once undergone by Vader himself. Although he continued to tend to the castle grounds, he eventually came to acknowledge that Darth Vader had truly died and would never again haunt the cooling plains of Mustafar.[[119]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vaneé-119)

#### Pathway to the Sith Eternal[]

:   "*I must warn you, our fiery planet burns away deception. If you proceed down this path, you will encounter your true self.*"
:   ―Eye of Webbish Bog, to Kylo Ren[[44]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-44)

 [![Mustafar was visited by Kylo Ren, Supreme Leader of the First Order, years after the death of his grandfather, Darth Vader.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fc/Steadfast-Mustafar-TROS.png/revision/latest?cb=20250214020300) [![Mustafar was visited by Kylo Ren, Supreme Leader of the First Order, years after the death of his grandfather, Darth Vader.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fc/Steadfast-Mustafar-TROS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/360?cb=20250214020300)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fc/Steadfast-Mustafar-TROS.png/revision/latest?cb=20250214020300) 

Mustafar was visited by Kylo Ren, Supreme Leader of the First Order, years after the death of his grandfather, Darth Vader.

 

After the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order") nearly destroyed the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance") at the [Battle of Crait](/wiki/Battle_of_Crait "Battle of Crait")[[2]](#cite_note-Galactic_Explorer's_Guide-2) in 34 ABY,[[132]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_Date-132) the faction's newly ascended [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") [Kylo Ren](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo") sought to rid himself of all connections to his past, including his maternal grandfather, Darth Vader.[[135]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-135) Knowing that Vader once ruled Mustafar, Ren had at a time regarded it as hallowed ground—the place where Anakin Skywalker died and a Dark Lord of the Sith was born.[[40]](#cite_note-TROS_JN-40) He traveled to Mustafar alone aboard [his TIE silencer](/wiki/Kylo_Ren%27s_TIE_silencer "Kylo Ren's TIE silencer") with the intent of destroying the legacy of Vader that remained on the planet. On this personal crusade, he encountered members of the Alazmec of Winsit[[135]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-135)—who deemed Ren unworthy of Mustafar's secrets[[134]](#cite_note-Alazmec_DB-134)—and slew them at the entrance of his grandfather's fortress. Inside he met Vaneé, who convinced Ren that his past could be used as a weapon, as even Vader had used his painful memories to deepen his connection to the dark side. The two departed Mustafar and traveled to Tatooine to uncover more of Ren's [family history](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family").[[135]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-135)

Around the same time, the [pirate](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") [Hondo Ohnaka](/wiki/Hondo_Ohnaka "Hondo Ohnaka") wrote about Mustafar in his [book](/wiki/Book "Book") *[Galactic Explorer's Guide](/wiki/Galactic_Explorer%27s_Guide "Galactic Explorer's Guide")*.[[2]](#cite_note-Galactic_Explorer's_Guide-2) Elsewhere, the confused [pilot](/wiki/Resistance_pilot "Resistance pilot") [Shriv Suurgav](/wiki/Shriv_Suurgav "Shriv Suurgav") uttered "what in the depths of Mustafar?" during his [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Bracca "Mission to Bracca") to acquire starfighters for the Resistance when [First Order stormtroopers](/wiki/First_Order_stormtrooper "First Order stormtrooper") he was fighting began to be hit by [arrows](/wiki/Arrow "Arrow") from the [Bracca resistance](/wiki/Bracca_resistance "Bracca resistance").[[136]](#cite_note-Resistance_Reborn-136)

In 35 ABY,[[43]](#cite_note-Timelines-43) the First Order [*Resurgent*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Resurgent-class_Star_Destroyer "Resurgent-class Star Destroyer") [*Steadfast*](/wiki/Steadfast_(Resurgent-class) "Steadfast (Resurgent-class)") arrived over Mustafar following a mysterious [broadcast](/wiki/Palpatine%27s_broadcast "Palpatine's broadcast") from the resurrected Darth Sidious.[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) Supreme Leader Ren had returned to the world once ruled by his grandfather, this time accompanied by the might of the [First Order Navy](/wiki/First_Order_Navy "First Order Navy"). Landing in his [TIE whisper](/wiki/TIE/wi_modified_interceptor "TIE/wi modified interceptor") with General [Armitage Hux](/wiki/Armitage_Hux "Armitage Hux") and [Allegiant General](/wiki/Allegiant_General "Allegiant General") [Enric Pryde](/wiki/Enric_Pryde "Enric Pryde") observing him from afar,[[44]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-44) Kylo Ren rallied his forces to Mustafar as part of his [search for answers](/wiki/Search_for_Exegol "Search for Exegol") to confront whoever was behind the transmission. The Supreme Leader and his stormtroopers [slaughtered](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar_(First_Order) "Mission to Mustafar (First Order)") what remained of the [cult](/wiki/Religion "Religion") of Alazmec colonists near the ruins of Vader's castle,[[137]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-137) who were sworn to protect the surrounding fen.[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) Afterward, Ren traveled through the fen and arrived at a small lake, where he encountered the Eye of Webbish Bog.[[44]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-44)

 [![Ren killed the Alazmec colonists before claiming the Sith wayfinder that once belonged to his grandfather.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/Kylo_Mustafar.png/revision/latest?cb=20200706075808) [![Ren killed the Alazmec colonists before claiming the Sith wayfinder that once belonged to his grandfather.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/Kylo_Mustafar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/320?cb=20200706075808)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/Kylo_Mustafar.png/revision/latest?cb=20200706075808) 

Ren killed the Alazmec colonists before claiming the Sith wayfinder that once belonged to his grandfather.

 

The Eye knew what Ren sought but warned him of encountering his "true self" if he were to continue down his current path. When Ren did not respond, the Eye relented and rewarded the Supreme Leader for his victory over the Alazmec, pointing the way to Vader's Sith wayfinder.[[44]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-44) Ren was guided by wisps of the dark side and came to an altar surrounded by the fortress ruins where he found the wayfinder.[[40]](#cite_note-TROS_JN-40) The Eye of Webbish Bog then disappeared into the lake, leaving Ren alone with the artifact. Knowing that he would not be the only one to travel to Mustafar in search of the object,[[44]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-44) Ren, with the word "Exegol" suddenly in his thoughts,[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) departed the planet with the rest of the First Order forces. The Eye's prophecy soon came true: Ren reached the planet Exegol, where he found the resurrected Sidious with his [Sith Eternal](/wiki/Sith_Eternal "Sith Eternal") followers, and eventually [returned](/wiki/Mission_to_Kef_Bir "Mission to Kef Bir") to abiding by the light side of the Force, joining the Jedi [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker") to [destroy](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol") Sidious once and for all, ending the [galactic war](/wiki/First_Order-Resistance_War "First Order-Resistance War").[[44]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-44)

After the destruction of Sidious at the Battle of Exegol, the [historian](/wiki/Historian "Historian") [Beaumont Kin](/wiki/Beaumont_Kin "Beaumont Kin") penned the [book](/wiki/Book "Book") *[The Rise and Fall of the Galactic Empire](/wiki/The_Rise_and_Fall_of_the_Galactic_Empire "The Rise and Fall of the Galactic Empire")*. In the book, Kin wrote about Mustafar's feared reputation and referenced the file titled "Mustafar" in the [Imperial Archives](/wiki/Imperial_Archives "Imperial Archives") section about Darth Vader.[[138]](#cite_note-Rise_and_Fall-138)

## Inhabitants[]

### The Mustafarians[]

:   "*Mustafar is our world. We have already lost so much. The lifefires barely burn. It is time to come together…and save what is left.*"
:   ―Father Kkkt[[20]](#cite_note-DV23-20)

 [![However harsh and volcanic, Mustafar was not devoid of life.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e6/KkktAttacksFortressVader-2017DarthVader23.png/revision/latest?cb=20181130031729) [![However harsh and volcanic, Mustafar was not devoid of life.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e6/KkktAttacksFortressVader-2017DarthVader23.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/350?cb=20181130031729)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e6/KkktAttacksFortressVader-2017DarthVader23.png/revision/latest?cb=20181130031729) 

However harsh and volcanic, Mustafar was not devoid of life.

 

Boasting a population of approximately 15,000[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) to 20,000 individuals,[[2]](#cite_note-Galactic_Explorer's_Guide-2) Mustafar was the [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") of the Mustafarians, a species primarily concerned with their own advancement and survival[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24) that lived in underground caves created by the lava fleas that ate through the planet's crust.[[31]](#cite_note-AEYNK-31) Two races of Mustafarians evolved in distinctly different cave systems[[15]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-15) in the mountains from extremophile arthropods,[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) [one subspecies](/wiki/Southern_Mustafarian "Southern Mustafarian") living near the planet's equator and the [other](/wiki/Northern_Mustafarian "Northern Mustafarian") in the north. They lived together as needed, although the geographical distance and limited desirable living space tended to limit the subspecies in their own communities.[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24)

Only venturing up to the surface in order to collect valuable minerals from the lava flows, the southern Mustafarians carried out the heavy labor involved due to[[31]](#cite_note-AEYNK-31) their short and strong physiology that developed due to the relatively higher gravity of their homeland, surviving high temperatures and frequent accidents on lava flows thanks to their thick carapaces, while the tall and slender northern Mustafarians had keen, faceted [eyes](/wiki/Eye "Eye") which easily spotted flaws in ore and machinery alike,[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24) and who acted as guards and expert riders of the lava flea, a creature that the natives made their armor from the heat-resistant shells of.[[31]](#cite_note-AEYNK-31)

Chitinous exoskeletons and low-[water](/wiki/Water "Water") biology allowed Mustafarians to withstand the intense heat of their homeworld, although they still required insulated clothes and breathing apparatus to work on the surface.[[13]](#cite_note-CL-13) The native Mustafarians developed and sought technology for survival more so than most other species, and some enhanced themselves with cybernetics to better carry out common tasks and withstand the harsh environments of their homeworld. Having learned from tragic experiences, Mustafarians did not trust imported technology until they themselves modified and adapted them to Mustafar's climes. While the two Mustafarian subspecies lived together as needed, the geographical distance and limited desirable living space tended to keep them in their own communities,[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24) although it was not unheard of for clans to be comprised of both northern and southern Mustafarians.[[42]](#cite_note-DV21-42)

 [![Mustafar's volcanic crust allowed for the creation of Mustafarian Lava Buns.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/54/Mustafarian_lava_buns.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200303020923) [![Mustafar's volcanic crust allowed for the creation of Mustafarian Lava Buns.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/54/Mustafarian_lava_buns.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/224?cb=20200303020923)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/54/Mustafarian_lava_buns.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200303020923) 

Mustafar's volcanic crust allowed for the creation of Mustafarian Lava Buns.

 

The Mustafarians grew few crops, as the lack of water meant traditional [farms](/wiki/Farm "Farm"), even when located underground, could not be sustained;[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24) water had to be imported to Mustafar.[[31]](#cite_note-AEYNK-31) Nevertheless, despite the what little life Mustafar had compared to other worlds, various types of edible fungi and domesticated herds of large insectoid creatures made up much of the Mustafarian diet, and unlike other hotbeds of industry in the galaxy, Mustafar was largely self-sufficient in regards to its food supply.[[24]](#cite_note-SM-24)

Southern Mustafarians made [Mustafarian Lava Buns](/wiki/Mustafarian_Lava_Bun "Mustafarian Lava Bun") by placing sweet balls of dough upon the planet's volcanic crust, heating it up to create a red bread with a cracked and blackened exterior. The [Artiodac](/wiki/Artiodac "Artiodac") [chef](/wiki/Chef "Chef") [Strono Tuggs](/wiki/Strono_Tuggs "Strono Tuggs") witnessed the production of the baked goods during a visit to Mustafar, learning the recipe to the buns in the process.
